kṛtam yasya ājñayā jagatsraṣṭā viriñciḥ pālakaḥ hāraḥ tīrthānām uttamam tīrtha kṣetrāṇām kṣetram uttamam munīnām āśrayaḥ nityam naimiṣa araṇyam uttamam śaunaka ādyāḥ mahātmānaḥ śiva bhaktāḥ mahā ojasaḥ tasmin sattre mahābhāgaḥ munīnām bhāgya gauravāt munīn draṣṭum sūtaḥ paurāṇika uttamaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā te mahātmānaḥ naimiṣa araṇya vāsinaḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ praśum udyuktāḥ papracchuḥ romaharṣaṇam ūcuḥ katham bhagavatā pūrvam ādityena ātma rūpiṇā purāṇam kathitam sauram tat naḥ vaktum iha arhasi tvayā tvattaḥ na asti paraḥ vaktā purāṇānām mahā tapas santi anye bahavaḥ śiṣyāḥ api tasya mahātmanaḥ tathā śiṣya vātsalyāt tvam purāṇeṣu yojitaḥ yāni anyāni purāṇāni tvayā uktāni mahā mune mad bhakti mṛte yasmāt muktiḥ na asti iti śuśruma devaḥ ayam bhagavān bhānuḥ antaryāmī sanātanaḥ yaḥ brūte sarva vastūnām tattvam jñātvā eva na anyathā atas śraddhā hi mahatī śrotum tvad vadana amṛtam naḥ vartate sūtam romaharṣaṇa suvrata taḥ uvāca natvā sūryaiḥ param dhām ṛc yajuḥ sāma rūpiṇam purāṇam saṃpravakṣyāmi sauram śiva kathā āśrayam yat śrutvā manujaḥ śīghram pāpa kañcukam utsṛjet paurāṇā vṛttim āśritya ye jīvanti dvijātayaḥ māhātmyam kathyate śambho na asti asmāt adhikam dvijāḥ idam purāṇam vaktavyam dhārmikāya anasūyave hānāya śiva eka atibuddhaye āsīt manuḥ sūrya sutaḥ vartate yaḥ mahā tapāḥ sa kadācid mahābhāgaḥ kāmika ākhyam vanam yayau tattvam vicārayāmāsuḥ mithas yatra mahā ṛṣayaḥ te mahābhāgāḥ bhṛgu ādyāḥ tattva nirṇaye evam sthiteṣu vipreṣu māyayā mohita ātmasu saṃśaya āviṣṭa citteṣu vāc abhūt aśarīriṇī śrutvā tu munayaḥ sarve bhṛgu ādyāḥ dagdha kilviṣāḥ mā enum puraskṛtya yayuḥ kṣetram vai dvādaśa ātmanaḥ viśrutam dvādaśādityam iti lokeṣu tat vijāḥ paśyantu mām param devam viśva antaryāmiṇam vibhum taḥ uvāca iti dṛṣṭvā ravim sākṣāt pratyakṣam puratas sthitam mene kṛtārtham ātmānam manuḥ vaivasvataḥ tadā saṃyamī nama namaḥ vareṇyāya vara dāya aṃśumāline triloka cakṣuṣe tubhyam triguṇāya amṛtāya ca nara nārī śarīrāya namaḥ te jñānāya akhila īśāya sapta aśvāya trimūrtaye namaḥ vyāhṛti rūpāya tri lakṣāya āśu gāmine eka lakṣa vilakṣāya bahu lakṣāya daṇḍine eka saṃsthā dvi saṃsthāya bahu saṃsthāya te namaḥ śakti trayāya śuklāya ravaye parameṣṭhine tvam śiva tvam hariḥ deva tvam brahmā tvam divaspatiḥ tvam akāraḥ vaṣaṭkāraḥ svadhā svāhā tvam eva hi tvām ṛte paramātmānam na tat paśyāmi daivatam munibhiḥ saha dharma ātmā samyak darśana kāṅkṣibhiḥ tasmin tu kim rūpam tasya jñānam kimātmakam caritam tasya kim tāta kim tīrtham tad adhiṣṭhitam lakṣaṇam ca purāṇānām vratānām ca kramaḥ yathā varṇānām āśramāṇām ca varṇa ācāra vidhiḥ katham śrāddham katham vā kriyate prāyaścitta vidhiḥ katham etat sarvam hi bhagavan pṛṣṭam vaktum iha arhasi evam manoḥ vacaḥ śrutvā bhagavān bhāskaraḥ dvijāḥ yat pṛṣṭam tat aśeṣeṇa vaktum samupacakrame iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde naimiṣāraṇyapraśaṃsādikathanam nāma prathamaḥ adhyāyaḥ bhānuḥ uvāca śṛṇu putra pravakṣyāmi tattvam yatra pratiṣṭhitam purāṇe asmin mahābhāgaiḥ sarva veda artha saṃgrahe tattvam yat bhagavantaḥ rūpam īśasya śūlinaḥ viśvam tena akhilam vyāptam na anyena iti abravīt śrutiḥ saḥ eva ātmā samastānām bhūtānām manuja adhipaiḥ caitanya rūpī bhagavant mahādevaḥ saha umayā bahudhā bhāti līlayā kevalaḥ śivaḥ brahma viṣṇu ādi rūpeṇa devadevaḥ maheśvaraḥ pṛṣṭaḥ brahma ādibhiḥ devaiḥ kaḥ tvam devaiḥ iti śaṃkaraḥ abravīt aham eva ekaḥ na anyaḥ kaścid iti śrutiḥ mahādevān līlā vigraha rūpiṇaḥ tam ekam paramātmānam ādi kartāram īśvaram prāhuḥ bahuvidham tad jñāḥ indram mitram iti śrutiḥ na tasmāt adhikaḥ kaścid na aṇīyāḥ api kaścana tena idam akhilam pūrṇaiḥ śaṃkareṇa mahātmanā mumukṣubhiḥ sadā dhyeyaḥ śivaḥ ekaḥ nirañjanaḥ harṣa ānanda rūpayā gauryā krīḍati sma maheśvaraḥ akṣeram paramam vyoma śaivam jyotiḥ anāmayam na anyaḥ vedyaḥ svayam jyotīḥ rudraḥ ekaḥ nirañjanaḥ tasmin jñāte akhilam jñātam iti āhuḥ veda vādinaḥ mama brahmā ca viṣṇuḥ śva śakraḥ ca anye divaukasaḥ adya api upāyaiḥ vividhaiḥ śambho darśana kāṅkṣiṇaḥ bhaktyā eva ananyayā rājñ jñāyate bhagavant śivaḥ bhargāt viśvasya bharaṇāt viśvayoneḥ umāpateḥ tasya jñāna mayī śaktiḥ avyayā girijā śivā mayoḥ bhedam ajñāḥ na paramārthāt māyā sā paramā śaktiḥ akṣa erā girijā avyayā māyā viśva ātmakaḥ rudra rata jñātvā hi amṛtī bhavet dharma artha kāma mokṣāṇām prāyaṇe kāraṇam param mahā bhaktiḥ sadā satyam na anya kiṃcana bhū tale trilokyām sukha kāmaḥ yaḥ tena pūjyaḥ sadāśivaḥ mṛte saukhyam kutas syāt dehinām mahā bhaktyā dhanam vidyā yaśaḥ tathā yadā lalāṭe sukha prāptiḥ likhitā bhavet sadā śiva sevāyām matiḥ bhavati iti veda siddhāntaḥ sva ātmani avasthitam devam viśva vyāpinam īśvaram bhaktyā paramayā rājñ jñātvā pāśaiḥ vimucyate saṃkalam tasya bhāsā eva bhāti na anyena śaṃkaraḥ tasmin prakāśamāne hi na eva bhānti anala ādayaḥ tasmin maheśvare gūḍhe vidyā avidye kṣara akṣare bhāti na vastutas tasmin jñāte akhilaiḥ pāśaiḥ mucyate manuja īśvaraḥ sarve krīḍanakāḥ tasya devadevasya śūlinaḥ ha ādi sarge mahādevaḥ brahmānam asṛjat prabhuḥ dakṣiṇa aṅgāt virūpākṣaḥ sṛṣṭi arthe līlayā kila asṛjat pālana artham ca vāma bhāgāt maheśvaraḥ hṛdayāt kālaiḥ rudra ākhyam jaga saṃhāra kārakam asṛjat yoginām dhyeyaḥ nirguṇaḥ tu svayam śivaḥ hi saṃbhūtam tasmin tiṣṭhati śaṃkare saḥ eva ātmā mahādevaḥ sarveṣām eva dehinām bhakti yuktena jñātavyaḥ parameśvaraḥ na paśyāmi mahādevāt adhikam devatā antaram api eva āhuḥ vedāḥ ūcuḥ yam prapaśyanti vidvāṃsaḥ yoginaḥ kṣapita āśayāḥ niyamya karaṇa grāmam saḥ eva ātmā maheśvaraḥ yasya prasādāt jīvanti saḥ devaḥ pārvatīpatiḥ na jānanti param bhāvam yasya brahma ādayaḥ surāḥ śṛṇvantu devatāḥ sarvāḥ satyam asmad vacaḥ param na asti rudrāt mahādevāt adhikam daivatam param na yathā kūrma romāṇi śṛṅgam na śaśa mastake mahādevam vijānīyāt deham asmi iti paṇḍitaḥ brāhmā nārāyaṇā raudrā pūjayitvā maheśvarīm yat prapaśyanti yogi indrāt tat vidyāt śāṃkaram padam kramāt cattrāṇi caṃkramya śaṅkhinyām upari sthitam deva yāna patham hitvā pitṛyāṇam tathā uttaram mukhaḥ janakaḥ sarva bhūtānām ekaḥ eva maheśvaraḥ mātram hṛd padme sthitam devam umāpatim ye anupaśyanti teṣām śāntiḥ hi śāśvatā pṛthivyām tiṣṭhati vibhuḥ pṛthivī vetti na eva tam rūpam ca pṛthivī yasya tasmai bhūmi ātmane namaḥ tiṣṭhati ameya ātmā na tam vetti kadācana sūrye tiṣṭhati yaḥ devaḥ na sūryaḥ vetti śaṃkaram yaḥ candre tiṣṭhati virbhuḥ candraḥ vetti na śāśvatam api pramāṇa padam ārūḍhāḥ tvad prasādāt vṛṣadhvajaiḥ bhānuḥ uvāca evam veda stutim śrutvā bhagavān girijāpatiḥ pratyakṣaḥ samabhūt teṣām vedānām manuja adhipaiḥ sūrya koṭi pratīkāśaḥ sahasra akṣaḥ sahasrapād sahasra śīrṣā puruṣaḥ sūrya soma agni locanaḥ sthūlāt sthūlataraḥ sthūlaḥ sūkṣmāt sūkṣmataraḥ paraḥ maheśvaraḥ uvāca mad prasādāt bhaviṣyadhvam he vedāḥ loka pūjitāḥ yuṣmān āśritya vipra indrāḥ karma kurvanti na anyathā niṣphalam tat bhavet karma teṣām tvad daivajñayā nityam naimittikam kāmyam yat ca anyat mokṣa sādhanam ye vai yuṣmān an ādṛtya śāstram kurvanti mānavāḥ tvad kṛtam param stotram ye paṭhiṣyanti vai dvijāḥ teṣām adhyayanam puṇyam mad prasādāt bhaviṣyati bhānuḥ uvāca akṣaram nirguṇam śuddham ānandam param avyayam pratyakṣam sarva bhūtānām ajñānām tad viparyayaḥ mahādevam jānīya ātmani saṃsthitam bhaktim āsthāya parama om param nirvāṇam āpnuhi tīrtha yātrāḥ bahuvidhāḥ yajñāḥ ca vividhāḥ kṛtāḥ yeṣām janma sahasreṣu teṣām bhaktiḥ bhavet śive tatra akṣayaḥ paraḥ dharmaḥ śiva dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ yajñāt tīrthāt japa ādānāt dharmaḥ syāt bahu sādhanaḥ sādhana prārthanā kleśaḥ para sampatti duḥkha daḥ saṃcitam janma sāhasraiḥ pāpam yadi te vijñeyāḥ mahātmānaḥ iti satyam bravīmi aham tad pādma kalpaiḥ samudbhūtām brahmanā samudīritām parayā rājñ śṛṇu tvam gadataḥ mama vakṣye aham tam bhuvana nāyakam māsīt ādye kṛta yuge sapta dvīpa eka ra āvaliḥ pratiṣṭhāna pure ramye gaṅgā tīre manorame tatra sthitvā akhilām pṛthvīm tasmin rājñi śāsati kadācid tatra bhagavān tṛṇabinduḥ mahā muniḥ ājagāma sa tam sudyumnam priya darśanam tam āyāntam munim dṛṣṭvā rājā rudra arcane rataḥ udvāsya āca mahā bāhuḥ utthāya ca kṛtāñjaliḥ bhagavān āgataḥ yasmāt mām draṣṭum muni sattamaiḥ bhānuḥ uvāca sudyumnasya vacaḥ śrutvā muniḥ āha mahā manāḥ tṛṇabinduḥ uvāca tathā api caritam śrutvā te aham vismaya anvitaḥ mahā bāho śrotum kautūhalam hi mama maheśvaraḥ idam puṇyam iti jñātvā kṛtam na anena yadi api māhara prahara ityādi nāma saṃkīrtanam ca yat karoti tena puṇyena duṣkṛtam bhasmasātkṛtam pāpa leśaḥ api na asya asti iti mama niścitā matiḥ suvyāḍim pūjayāmāsa yathāvat vidhi pūrvakam sūryātapratīkāśam divya strībhiḥ virājitam deva dūtaiḥ samānītam āruhya muni puṃgavaiḥ tatra bhuktvā mahā bhogān yugānām ayutam tatas tatas tu karmaṇaḥ śeṣam bhoktum atra mahī tale smarāmi pūrvakām jātim prasādāt śūlinaḥ mune maheśasya māhātmyam paramātmanaḥ yasya nāmnaḥ phalam idam ajñāna uccāraṇāt api jñātvā yaḥ kīrtayet śam bhoḥ nāmāni amita tejasaḥ bhānuḥ uvāca iti sarvam aśeṣeṇa caritam tasya dhīmataḥ muniḥ śrutvā vismitaḥ abhūt punar punar mahātmānam rāja puṃgavam rāja svam āśrama padam yāmi iti uktvā jagāma saḥ iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure bhānumanusaṃvāde sudyunnākhyānam nāma tṛtīyaḥ adhyāyaḥ rājñaḥ sakāśāt sa muniḥ matvā kim kṛtavan punar bhānuḥ uvāca revā tīre mahat puṇyam jāleśvaram iti smṛtam muni siddha niṣevitam tīrtha yātrām cakāra saḥ kāni tīrthāni guhyāni yeṣu saṃnihitaḥ śivaḥ bhānuḥ uvāca tīrthānām uttamam tīrtham kṣetrāṇām kṣetram uttamam mārāṇasī iti nagarī priyā devasya śulinaḥ yatra viśveśvaraḥ devaḥ sarveṣām iha dehinām dadāti tārakam jñānam saṃsārāt mocakam param yatra sarva pāpānām dṛṣṭā spṛṣṭā namaskṛtā na asti gaṅgā samam tīrthe vārāṇasyām viśeṣataḥ kim tat śreyaskaram iti hṛdi kṛtvā jagāma saḥ nandīśvarasya yaḥ śiṣyaḥ yoginām agraṇī svayam xcā deva gaṇa ākīrṇe yakṣa gandharva sevite siddha siddha cāraṇa kūṣmāṇḍaiḥ apsarobhiḥ ca saṃkule gaṅgā mandākinī yatra rājate duḥkha hāriṇī tasya āśramam anuprāpya pārāśaryaḥ mahā muniḥ abhivādya yathānyāyam tasya agre upaviśya ca tāñjali puṭaḥ bhūtvā vākyam etat uvāca ha prāptam kali yugam ghoram puṇya mārga bahiṣkṛtam pākhaṇḍa ācāra niratam mleccha antra jana saṃkulam adhārmikāḥ krūraiḥ sattvāḥ dhanācīra alpa medhasaḥ tasmin yuge bhaviṣyanti brāhmaṇāḥ śūdra yājakāḥ snānam deva arcanam dānam homam ca pitṛ tarpaṇam svādhyāyam na kariṣyanti brāhmaṇāḥ hi kalau yuge na paṭhanti tathā vedān śreyase brāhmaṇa adhamāḥ pratigraha artham vedān ca paṭhiṣyanti kalau yuge puruṣottamam āśritya śiva nindā ratāḥ dvijāḥ bhaviṣyanti teṣām trātā na mādhavaḥ svām svām vṛttim parityajya para vṛtti upajīvakāḥ brāhmaṇa ādyāḥ bhaviṣyanti saṃprāpte tu kalau yuge etān pāpa ratān dṛṣṭvā rājān aśva avicārakāḥ bhaviṣyanti kalau prāpte vṛthak jāti abhimāninaḥ ucca āsana gatāḥ śūdrāḥ dṛṣṭvā ca brāhmaṇān tadā pāṣāyaṇaḥ ca nirgranthāḥ nagnāḥ kāpālikāḥ tathā tapaḥ yajña phalānām tu vikretāraḥ dvija adhamāḥ yatayaḥ ca bhaviṣyanti śataśas atha sahasraśas tad bhaktān ca mahātmnaḥ brāhmaṇān ca kalau yuge tāḍay durātman brāhmaṇa rājan sevaka na nivārayate rājā tān dṛṣṭvā api kalau yuge gaccha vārāṇasīm vyāsaiḥ yatra viśveśvaraḥ śivaḥ ucyate yasmin dṛṣṭe kṣaṇāt jantuḥ saṃsāram na punar viśet gatvā paiśyaiḥ param liṅgam tatra satyavatī suta snātvā gaṅgā jale puṇye paśya viśveśvaram param sa dāsyati param jñānam yena muktaḥ bhaviṣyasi dṛṣṭvā viśveśvaram devam yāvat tiṣṭhati tad kṣaṇāt āgamiṣyanti munayaḥ tvām draṣṭum sarve eva te brūhi mad vacanāt teṣām jñānam māheśvaram param evam satyavatī sūnuḥ tad māhātmyam aśeṣatas sanatkumārāt sva guroḥ śrutvā māheśvara agraṇī sa śiṣyaḥ prayayau śīghram vyāsaḥ vārāṇasīm prati gatvā vārāṇasīm vyāsaḥ siddha ṛṣi muni sevitām bhānuḥ uvāca saṃprāpya kāśīm dharma ātmā kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ muniḥ snātvā yathāvat jāhnavyām tarpayitvā surān pitan yayau viśveśvaram draṣṭum jyotiḥ liṅgat manāmayam saṃpūjya sarva bhāvena daṇḍa vat praṇipatya ca devasya dakṣiṇā mūrtau upaviśya mahā muniḥ paśyan viśveśvaram liṅgam jaipan vai śatarudriyam hi kṣaṇāt liṅgāt param jyotiḥ āvirbhūtam nirañjanam sūkṣmāt sūkṣmam ca paramam ānandam tamasaḥ param yat tat māheśvaram jyotiḥ vedānteṣu pratiṣṭhitam darśanāt tasya ca muneḥ pārāśaryasya dhīmataḥ divyam māheśvaram jñānam udbhūtam kevalam śivam advayam nirguṇam śāntam jīvanmuktaḥ tadā muniḥ yasmin dṛṣṭe kṣaṇāt jñānam uditam mama nirmalam namaḥ bhagavante te viśvanāthāya śūline durvijñeya aprameyāya paramānanda rūpiṇe bhakti priyāya sūkṣmāya pārvatīśāya te namaḥ jānāti api na jānanti bhānuḥ uvāca mā asīt vṛṣadhvajaḥ tatas tam abravīt vākyam kāruṇyāt śubhayā girā vyāsaḥ uvāca bhagavant kṛtakṛtyaḥ asmi darśanāt te śaṃkaraiḥ tvad viṣayam jñānam devānām api durlabham dehi me devadeveśaiḥ na anyat iṣṭam varam mama bhānuḥ uvāca varam dattvā muni indrāya kṣaṇāt antarhitaḥ abhavat tasmāt ṭhyāsāt paraḥ na anyaḥ śiva bhaktaḥ jagāye bhagavant vā devakī sūnuḥ arjunaḥ vā mahāmatiḥ evam harāt labdha varaḥ kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ tatra yāni ca liṅgāni tāni draṣṭum yayau muniḥ iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure bhānu ganusaṃvāde mahādeva varadānam nāma pañcamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ kāni divyāni liṅgāni yāni draṣṭum yayau muniḥ māhātmyam ca api kṛtsnaśas taḥ uvāca yat uktam bhānunā pūrvam manave muni sattamāḥ tat eva kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇudhvam gadataḥ mama māgneyyām avimuktasya vāpī trailokya viśrutā yatra saṃnihitāḥ davaḥ nityam viśveśvaraḥ śivaḥ yatra snānam dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ devānām api durlabham teṣām liṅgāni jāyante hṛdaye trīṇi suvratāḥ tatra satyavatī sūnuḥ khātvā ca eva yathāvidhi yayau tatra brahma ādayaḥ devāḥ sevante śūlapāṇinam tasya darśana mātreṇa jñānam pāśupatam bhavet jagāma saḥ muniḥ paśu ādraṣṭum vai tārakeśvaram yatra anta kāle bhagavant jñānam tat saṃprayacchati tat dṛṣṭvā paramam liṅgam vyāsaḥ satyavatī sutaḥ yayau śukreśvaram draṣṭum sarva siddhi pradāyakam ārādhya muninā yatra śukreṇa amita tejasā prāptā saṃjīvanī vidyā surāṇām api durlabhā tasmin kūpe muniḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā śukreśvaram śivam brahmeśvaram yayau draṣṭum tatra brahmā virāj svayam tapaḥ taptvā mahā ghoram prītaye pārvatīpateḥ brahmatvam prāptavan brahmā yogam ca anye mahā ṛṣayaḥ yatra sākṣāt śivaḥ sūkṣmaḥ nityam tiṣṭhati vai dvijāḥ anugrahāya lokānām paśu pāśa vimocakaḥ yatra pāśupatāḥ siddhāḥ oṃkāra īśvaram īśvaram saṃpūjya paramām siddhim prāsavantaḥ dvijottamāḥ tasmin liṅaḥ upoṣitaḥ idam ślokaḥ ghaṅancha saṃjñita pustakeṣu na asti yadi jāgaraṇam kuryāt param siddhim avāpnuyāt tatas satyavatī sūnuḥ kṛttivāsa īśvaram yayau upāsate mahādevam yatra brahma ādayaḥ surāḥ munayaḥ śaṃsita ātmānaḥ rudra jāpya parāyaṇāḥ dvijāḥ snātvā tatra mahādevam kṛttivāsa īśvaram śivam sakṛt paśyati yaḥ bhaktyā kṛttivāsa īśvaram vibhum haṃsatīrthe naraḥ snātvā kṛttivāseśvaram vibhum saṃpūjya parayā bhaktyā kṛttivāsa īśvaram śivam na patati eva saṃsāre na atra kāryā vicāraṇā yayau ratneśvaram draṣṭum mokṣaḥ yatra pratiṣṭhitaḥ yaḥ ayam pāśupataḥ yogaḥ paśu pāśa vimocakaḥ varṣeḥ dvādaśabhiḥ samyak kṛte pāśupate dvijāḥ ratneśvaram tu saṃpūjya pārāśaryaḥ mahā muniḥ draṣṭum deva adhideveśam vṛddhakāleśvaram yayau tasmāt liṅga mahādevaḥ sadā tiṣṭhati līlayā anugrahāya lokānām ayā saha viśvabhuj pṛthivyām yāni liṅgāni santi divyāni vai dvijāḥ vṛddhakāleśvare dṛṣṭe dṛṣṭāni eva na saṃśayaḥ devasya pūrva digbhāge kūpa om muni niṣevitaḥ pūritaḥ puṇya salilaiḥ devadevena śambhunā yaiḥ pītam tasya salilam prākṛtaiḥ culuka trayam tatra dvaipāyanaḥ viprāḥ snānam kṛtvā samāhitaḥ buddha kāla īśvara liṅgam saṃpūjya ca tatas yayau madhyameśvara nāmānam mokṣa liṅgam anuttamam upāsate param liṅgam śiva darśana kāṅkṣiṇaḥ mandākinyām muniḥ snātvā dṛṣṭvā vai madhyameśvaram ghaṇṭākarṇa snātvā liṅga tat vimalam śivam pratiṣṭhāpya muni śreṣṭhaḥ labdhavan jñānam uttamam dṛṣṭvā vyāseśvaram śivam yatra yatra mṛtaḥ vā api vārāṇasyām mṛtaḥ bhavet tatas satyavatī sūnuḥ kapardī īśvaram īśvaram draṣṭum jagāma dipa indrāḥ liṅgam tat pārameśvaram ye drakṣyanti kapardīśam kṛtārthāḥ te na saṃśayaḥ mānuṣām tanum āśritya rudrāḥ eva na saṃśayaḥ tasmin tīrthe muniḥ snātvā saṃtarpya ca surān pitṝn muniḥ yad yad yad yad yad tad tad tad tad tad tad tad tad tad tad adhyāya vārāṇasī liṅga pahima varṇanam nāma ṣaṣṭhaḥ adhyāyaḥ taḥ uvāca punar jagāma bhagavān kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ prabhuḥ dakṣeśvaram devam bhaktānām siddhi dāyakam yat śiva avajñayā pāpam jātam dakṣa prajāpateḥ tasya pāpasya mokṣāya tasmāt liṅge dvijottamāḥ mārādhya devadeveśam bahūni abda śatāni vai nidhāya dakṣaḥ prācetasaḥ yajñam akarot jāhnavī taṭe tasmin yajñe samāhūtāḥ indra ādyāḥ devatā gaṇāḥ bhagavantaḥ munayaḥ siddhāḥ rājānaḥ prathita ojasaḥ brahmā ca viṣṇunā sārdham āhūtaḥ tena dhīmatā devān sarvān ca bhāga artham ahūtān padmasaṃbhavaḥ dṛṣṭvā śivena rahitān dakṣam prati evam abravīt aho dakṣa mahā mūṃḍha durbuddhe kim kṛtam tvayā devāḥ sarve samāhūtāḥ śaṃkareṇa vinā katham antaryāmī sa viśveśaḥ sarveṣām eva dehinām bhoktā saḥ sarva yajñānām śaṃkaraḥ paramārthāt ete ca munayaḥ sarve tava sāhāyya kāriṇaḥ na jānanti param bhāvam mahādevasya śūlinaḥ ete ca devāḥ śakra ādyāḥ āgatāḥ yajña bhāginaḥ tad māyā mohitāḥ sarve na jānanti pinākinam dharma adharma vyavasthā ca varṇāḥ ca eva ca tiṣṭhanti śāsanāt tasya devadevasya śūlinaḥ sā ca śaktiḥ parā gaurī sva icchā vigraha cāriṇī kaḥ tām jānāti viśveśīm īśvara ardha śarīriṇīm aham na adya api jānāmi cakrī śakrasya kā kathā sva icchā vigraha rūpinyā gauryā saha pināka dhṛt bhrāmayati akhilam viśvam iti satyam na saṃśayaḥ saḥ eva badhnāti paśūn asmat ādīn maheśvaraḥ saḥ eva mocakaḥ devaḥ paśūnām naḥ iti śrutiḥ nāma saṃkīrtanāt yasya bhidyate pāpañjaram mama avajñā yatra āsste sthātavyam na eva sūribhiḥ taḥ uvāca dadhīciḥ abravīt akṣam munīnām agraṇī svayam uvāca katham deva adhideva īśaḥ karma sākṣī sanātanaḥ viśveśvaraḥ mahādevaḥ tvayā dakṣaiḥ na pūjyate anugraham vinā tasya katham jānāti śūlinam prasaṅgāt kautukāt lobhāt bhayāt ajñānāt api vā aho dakṣa tava ajñānam te nāśasya kāraṇam evam dadhīceḥ vacanam śrutvā dakṣaḥ vicakṣaṇaḥ dadhīcim abravīt viprāḥ śakra ādīnām ca saṃnidhau dakṣaḥ uvāca na aham nārāyaṇāt devāt paśyāmi anyam dvijottamaiḥ sarva vastūnām su niścitam uvāca saḥ eva kāraṇam na anyaḥ viṣṇoḥ api hi vai śrutiḥ yajñasya pālakaḥ viṣṇuḥ iti yat niścitam tvayā bhaviṣyati anyathā eva āśu paśyataḥ kamalāpateḥ ete ca brāhmaṇāḥ sarve ye dviṣā enti maheśvaram pāpaṇḍa ācāra niratāḥ sarve niraya gāminaḥ tu saṃprāpte daridrāḥ śūdra yājakāḥ sarvasmāt adhikaḥ rudraḥ paśu pāśa vimocakaḥ parāṅmukhaḥ tu vaḥ mā dijyā karā gatiḥ sva āśramam munibhiḥ juṣṭam oṃkāram narmadā taṭe dakṣa yajñasya vṛttāntam śrutvā devaṛṣeḥ mukhāt māha viśva adhikam rudram nirīkṣyamāṇam deveśī parānanda eka vigraham yaḥ ayam prācetasaḥ dakṣaḥ pitā me pūrva janmani nau avajñāya katham yajñam kartum pracakrame devāḥ sarve samāhūtāḥ viṣṇunā saha śaṃkaraiḥ raṇāḥ bhavanti siddhāḥ daiteyāḥ dānavāḥ ca ye rājānaḥ ca mahābhāgāḥ gandharvāḥ kiṃnarāḥ tathā avajñā kāriṇaḥ tasya yajñam śīghram vināśaya evam devyāḥ vacaḥ śrutvā devadevaḥ pinākadhṛt tad kṣaṇāt śambhu vīrabhadram mahā balam sahasra bāhum jaṭilam duṣṭānām ca bhayaṃkaram bhaktānām vara dam devam sūrya soma agni locanam umā kopa udbhavā devī bhadrakālī bhayaṃkarā anyāḥ ca devyaḥ rudrāḥ ca śataśas roma sambhavaḥ bhadrakālyā saha tadā vīrabhadraḥ mahā balaḥ gatvā sa yajñam dakṣasya bhasmasāt akarot vijāḥ dakṣaḥ tat adbhutam karma dṛṣṭvā atha bhaya vihvalaḥ mataḥ tat śaraṇam śīghram vīrabhadrasya śūlinaḥ uvāca vīrabhadraḥ tam dakṣam prācetasam dvijāḥ tasya pāpa vimokṣāya kāruṇya amṛta vāridhiḥ gaccha vārāṇasīm dakṣa sarva pāpa praṇāśinīm tad anugraha artham lokānām yatra tiṣṭhati śaṃkaraḥ anena eva śarīreṇa tatra mokṣam gamiṣyasi taḥ uvāca mahāmatiḥ sarva pratiṣṭhāpya mahā liṅga gaṅgā tīre manorame mārādhya parayā bhaktyā tasmāt liṅge layam gataḥ dakṣeśvarasya māhātmyam kathitam muni puṃgavāḥ trilocanasya māhātmyam sāṃpratam varṇyate mayā iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde dakṣeśvaramāhātmyādikathanam nāma saptamaḥ adhyāyaḥ taḥ uvāca trilocanāt param liṅgam vārāṇasyām na dṛśyate dṛṣṭāni eva bhavanti eva dṛṣṭe liṅgaiḥ trilocane asaṃkhyātāni pāpāni jñānāt ajñānāt api vā tāni nāśayati evam devadevaḥ trilocanaḥ māyā pāśena baddhānām sarveṣām prāṇinām api paścima abhimukham liṅgam sarpa mekhala maṇḍitam tasya darśana mātreṇa koṭi liṅga arcanam phalam trilocanam su saṃpūjya kṛṣṇadvaipāyanaḥ muniḥ yayau kāmeśvaram draṣṭum siddha liṅgam anuttamam prasannaḥ vividhāḥ siddhīḥ sarveṣām api durlabhāḥ teṣām kṛtānām kriyamāṇānām sarveṣām tapasām api tasya dakṣiṇa digbhāge kāmakuṇḍam iti smṛtam tatra snātvā naraḥ bhaktyā dṛṣṭvā kāmeśvaram śivam anyāni api ca liṅgāni vārāṇasyām sthitāni api saṃkhyām api na jānāti teṣām deva vaturmukhaḥ kaḥ vā vadati māhātmyam ṛte devāt maheśvarāt nandīśvaraḥ vā jānāti prasādāgirijā pateḥ atha satyavatī sūnu draṣṭum devīm śivām parām viśāla akṣā dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ yatra saṃnihitā śivā tām dṛṣṭvā vidhivat bhaktyā saṃpūjya ca mahā muniḥ parīnanda ātmakām gaurīm stutim matvā cakāra saḥ tvam eva mātā sarveṣām brahma ādīnām divaukasām ṛjuḥ kuṇḍalinī sukṣmā yoga siddhi pradāyinī svāhā svadhā mahāvidyā meghāḥ lakṣmī sarasvatī satī dākṣāyaṇī vidyā sarva śakti mayā śivā tathā ca ekaikapāṭalā umā haimavatī ca api kalyāṇī caitra mātṛkā khyātiḥ prajñā mahābhāgā loke gaurī iti viśrutā gaṇa ambikā mahādevī nandinī jātavedasī sāvitrī vara dā puṇyā pāvanā loka viśrutā niyatī raudrī durgā bhadrā pramāthinī gautamī kauśikī ca assrthā caṇḍī kātyāyanī satī mahā dhvajā śūla dharā paramā brahmacāriṇī mahendra upendra mātā ca pārvatī siṃhavāhanā evam stutvā viśāla akṣā divyaiḥ tebhiḥ su nāmbhiḥ takṛtyaḥ abhavat vyāsaḥ vārāṇasyām dvijottamāḥ yaḥ paśyati viśāla akṣām snātvā gaṅgā ambhasi dvijāḥ yaḥ paṭhet śṛṇuyāt vā api yāti māheśvaram padam iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde trilocana māhātmya ādi kathanam namāmaḥ adhyāyaḥ vac kim lakṣaṇam purāṇānām teṣām dānena kim phalam anyeṣām api dānānām vratānām ca viśeṣataḥ varṇānām āśramāṇām ca teṣām vai lakṣaṇam yathā tatas śrāddha vidhānam ca prāyaścittam katham bhavet mātsyam ca gāruḍam proktam brahmāṇḍam ca tatas param bhāga dvayena kathitam brahmāṇḍam ati saṃjñitam yāni ca uktāni sūribhiḥ saṃhitā dvaya saṃyuktam puṇyam śiva kathā āśrayam māyā sanatkumāra uktā dvitīyā sūrya bhāṣitā iyam puṇyatamā khyātā saṃhitā pāpa nāśinī dānam asya purāṇasya dānānām uttamam dvijāḥ yāni dānāni lokeṣu prasiddhāni dvijottamāḥ sarveṣām phalam āpnoti caturdaśyām na saṃśayaḥ brāhmam purāṇam prathamam dadāti śraddhayā anvitaḥ baiṣṇavam viṣṇum uddiśya dvādaśyām prayataḥ śuciḥ anūcānāya yaḥ dadyāt vaiṣṇavam padam āpnuyāt dadāti sūrya bhaktāya yaḥ tu bhāgavatam dvijāḥ tasyām tithau saṃyata ātmā brāhmaṇāya āhita āśaye bhaviṣya ākhyam purāṇam tu dadāti śraddhayā anvitaḥ markaṇḍeyam tu yaḥ dadyāt saptabhyām prayata ātmavān yajñasya phalam bhavati śāśvatam dadāti nāradīyam yaḥ caturdaśyām samāhitaḥ kārtikasya caturdaśyām śukla pakṣasya suvaitāḥ dā dvijendra śiva arcana ram vai dvādaśyām saṃyataḥ bhūtvā brāhmaṇāya tapasvine yaḥ vai dadāti vārāham viṣṇu lokam sa gacchati skāndam śivacaturdaśyām pradadyāt śvi yogine jñānī bhavati vipra indrāḥ mahādeva prasādāt dvādaśyām vā caturdaśyām dadyāt vāmanam uttamam mātsyam dadyāt dvijendrāya prayati ittarāyaṇe uddiśya dadyāt śvi tithau dvijāḥ hi śivasya puratas bhaktyā saṃprāpte dakṣiṇāyane gaṇa ādhipatyam ānoti devadevasya śūlinaḥ evam uktaḥ purāṇānām kramaḥ dānena yat phalam taḥ uvāca dānam pātre pradātavyam na apātre api aṇu mātrakam pātra bhūtān pravakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvam muni puṃgavāḥ dānena māpnuyāt saukhyam rūpam kānti yaśaḥ balam dānena śatrūn jayati vyādhiḥ dānena naśyati ādānāya sat pātram vicārya eva prayatnāt veda vedāṅga tatva jñāḥ śāntāḥ ca eva jita indriyāḥ śrauta smārta kriyā niṣṭhāḥ satya niṣṭhāḥ kuṭumbinaḥ tapasvi nara tīrtha tāḥ kṛtajñāḥ mita bhāṣiṇaḥ guru śuśrūṣaṇaiḥ atāḥ svādhyāya śīlinaḥ mahādeva arcana ratāḥ bhūtiśāsana bhūṣitāḥ uttamaḥ sarva pātrāṇām taramaiḥ dattam tat akṣayam tasmāt pāyatamam jñātvā śiva bhaktam akalmaṣam proktam naimittikam dānam ṛṣibhiḥ veda vādibhiḥ putra artham vā dhana artha vā svarga artham vā anyatas api vā dānam tat vimalam proktam kevalam mokṣa sādhanam yat kiṃcid īyate dānam daridrāya viśeṣataḥ su alpām api mahīm yaḥ tu dadāti śraddhayā anvitaḥ sa yāti brahmasadanam yatra devaḥ svayam virāj mahīm api gocarma mātrām yaḥ dadāti śraddhayā anvitaḥ śiva bhaktāya śāntāya sarva pāpaiḥ pramucyate na bhūmi dānāt adhikam dānam asti iha bhū tale hi daridrāya dattam bhavati ca akṣayam na eva dātavyam bhūmi dānam viśeṣataḥ yaiḥ dattāḥ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ ca grāmāḥ parama dhārmikaiḥ gṛhṇanti ye karam teṣu lobha andhāḥ pāpinaḥ nṛpāḥ tad ante makṣikāḥ yūkāḥ matkuṇāḥ maśakāḥ tathā kṛmayaḥ jālapāda arthe śūkarāḥ pakṣiṇaḥ tathā mad godhāḥ śaśāḥ sedhāḥ gardabha aśva pipīlikāḥ mūṣakāḥ kṛkalāsāḥ ca vṛkṣa gulma ādayaḥ tathā na teṣām niṣkṛtiḥ daṣṭā prāyaścitta śataiḥ api brahma hā śuddhim ānoti kālena muni puṃgavāḥ dvija grāma kara grāhī na eva śuddhim avāpnuyāt maidānakara ādānāt adhikam na asti pātakam dānānām uttamam dānam vidyā dānam viduḥ budhāḥ tat ca dānam vinītāya varṇa āśrama ratāya ca brāhmaṇāya eva śāntāya śuśrūṣaṇa ratāya ca anna dānam praśaṃsanti viduṣaḥ veda vādinaḥ anam eva yatas prāṇāḥ prāṇa dāna samam hi tat a parīkṣya eva sarvebhyaḥ iti svāyambhu śāsanāt mītaḥ ca bhagavān ranena eva śacīpatiḥ tasmāt viśiṣṭam tadā iyam āhuḥ veda vidaḥ budhāḥ na adhvagāya niṣiddham tat iti devaḥ abravīt raviḥ jīvanam sarva bhūtānām jalam eva dvijottamāḥ tiladaḥ putram āproti vāsodaḥ kāntim uttamām dīpadī nirmalām dṛṣṭim yāna daḥ śriyam uttamām mad śayyā pradaḥ śvā api tathā dhānya daḥ saukhyam uttamam tena dānena mahatā sāyujyam brahmanaḥ smṛtam gṛhītvā vetanam vedam yaḥ adhyāpayati mūḍha dhīḥ adhīte yaḥ hi vā dattvā tau ubhau pāpinī smṛtau surā bhāṇḍa gatam toyam yathā bhavati ninditam yāni bhojyāni mūlāni phalāni vividhāni ca śākāni brāhmaṇebhyaḥ ca dattvā atyantam sukhī bhavet indhanānām pradānena jāṭhara agni pradīpanam roga hīnaḥ sa dīrgha āyūḥ sukhī bhavati sarvadā gām alaṃkṛtya yaḥ dadyāt sa vatsām ca sa dakṣiṇām ṣoḍaśa ṛtavaḥ ye ca dānam tīrtheṣu yat smṛtam tat akṣayam bhavet dānam yogine ca viśeṣataḥ saṃkrānti ādiṣu kāleṣu dattam bhavati ca akṣayam mad śivam uddiśya yat dattam svalpam vā yadi vā bahu mahā ālaye viśeṣeṇa dattam bhavati ca akṣayam viśākha ṛkṣeṇa saṃyuktā vaiśākhī pūrṇimā bhavet tasyām tithau tu saṃpūjya brāhmaṇān sapta pañca vā tilaiḥ kṛṣṇaiḥ eva tilaiḥ vidvāḥ madhunā vā api upoṣitaḥ dharmarājaḥ yamaḥ śaktitas yāvajjīvam kṛtaiḥ pāpaiḥ kāyikaiḥ vā manogataiḥ mucyate tad kṣaṇāt eva dharmarāja prasādāt tilān kṛtvā hiraṇyam madhu sarpiṣī gām annam udakumbham ca vaiśākhyām saṃprayacchati yā śiva tithiḥ mādhe kṛṣṇa caturdaśī dadāti hema vāsaḥ vā phalam dhānyam atha api vā abhayam sarva bhūtebhyaḥ dadyāt dānam param smṛtam paṭhet yaḥ śṛṇuyāt vā api go dānasya phalam labhet iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī sore sūta śonaka saṃvāde dānāha vimādikathanam nāma daśamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca anyat vratam idam vakṣye śṛṇudhvam sunieṅgavāḥ maheśvareṇa kathitam sākṣāt svayam skandāya pṛcchate tad devadevaiḥ mahādevaiḥ śaśāṅka kṛta śekhara bhargaiḥ viśveśvara īśānaiḥ kāruṇya amṛta vāridhe kasya prasīdati kṣipram kena vā jñāyate bhavān yogaḥ tvad viṣayaḥ kaḥ vā jñānam tvad vipayam ca uvāca sarva āśī sarva bhakṣī vā sarva ācāra vilopakaḥ mad paraḥ vāmanaḥ kāyaiḥ muktaḥ eva na saṃśayaḥ tuṣṭaḥ aham bhakti leśena kṣipram yacche param padam tripuṇḍra dhārī satatam śāntaḥ rudra akṣa kaṅkaṇaḥ bhaktānām uttamaḥ vaiṣṇavaḥ paraḥ vaiṣṇavānām sahastrebhyaḥ śiva bhaktaḥ viśiṣyate yadi pāpa rataḥ krūraḥ sva āśrama ācāra varjitaḥ sam dambham samāśritya bhaktānām upajīvikāḥ saṃsārāt te api mucyante kim punar mad pare janāḥ mad bhaktānām ca māhātmyam kaḥ vā jānāti tattvāt tvam ca jānāsi nandī jānāti vā guha mārga sthaḥ vā api amārga sthaḥ mūrkhaḥ vā praṇḍitaḥ api vā sa vaḥ smin pustake caturdaśa adhyāya sthāne saṃgṛhītaḥ advaitam ekam parasam ātmānam jñāna vigraham paśyanti jñāninaḥ tu ekam ātma rūpam idam jagant aham ātmā vibhuḥ śuddhaḥ sphaṭika upala saṃnibhaḥ upādhi rahitaḥ śāntaḥ svayam jyotiḥ prakāśakaḥ ātmani eva akhilam bhāti śuktikā rajatam yathā mukti tattva parijñānāt tad nāśaḥ tadvat ātmani na tena lipyate hi ātmā puṇya apuṇya ākhya karmaṇā buddhi ādayaḥ guṇāḥ sarve bhūt buddheḥ akṛtiḥ ahaṃkārāt ca sūkṣmāṇi tanmātrāṇi indriyāṇi ca sūkṣmebhyaḥ pañca bhūtāni tebhyaḥ sthūlam idam jagat caturviṃśakam avyaktam puruṣaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ na tasya kārya karaṇam kriyā rūpam ca vidyate sva ajñānāt kathitam sarvam ātmani eva iti ca śrutiḥ iti mad viṣayam jñānam kathitam te putrakaiḥ nāma ekādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ maheśvaraḥ uvāca tasya pravakṣyāmi adhunā śṛṇu yamāḥ ca niyamāḥ tāvat āsanāni api ṣaṣ mukham prāṇāyāmaḥ tatas proktaḥ pratyāhāraḥ ca dhāraṇā dhyānam tathā samādhiḥ ca yoga aṅgāni pracakṣate māḥ saṃkṣepāt proktāḥ niyamān śṛṇu putrakaiḥ toṣaḥ śaucam īśvara pūjanam sarveṣām eva bhūtānām akleśa jananam hi yat tathā artha kathanam satyam asteyam adhunā śṛṇu vauryeṇa vā balena api para sva haraṇam ca yam mānānām api anādānam āpadi api yathā icchayā vāndrāyaṇa ādinā yat tu śarīrasya ca śoṣaṇam uttapaḥ kathitam putra svādhyāyam adhunā śṛṇu ha ṇavaḥ śatarudrīyam tathā atharvaśiraḥ śikhā eteṣām yaḥ japaḥ putra svādhyāyaḥ iti kīrtitaḥ tuṣṭaḥ saṃtoṣaḥ iti paṭhyate bāhye ca abhyantare ca api śuddhiḥ śaucam vidhīyate stuti smaraṇa pūjābhiḥ vāc manas kāya karmabhiḥ mayi bhaktiḥ dṛḍhā putraḥ etat īśvara pūjanam yamāḥ ca niyamāḥ proktāḥ saṃkṣepāt na tu vistarāt daṇḍa tākṣya āsanam śūlam kharga mudgaram eva ca makaram tripatham kāṣṭham sthāṇuḥ vā hasti karṇikam bhīmam vīrāsanam ca api vārāham mṛga vaiṇikam iti etāni āsanāni atra saptaviṃśati saṃkhyayā dvitīyaḥ sajayaḥ proktaḥ dhruvam vyāhṛtimātṛbhiḥ recakaḥ śūnyakaḥ ca eva pūrakaḥ kumbhakaḥ tathā evam caturvidhaḥ bhedaḥ prāṇāyāme atra sūribhiḥ asūnām nāḍayaḥ proktāḥ gama āgama laya āśrayāḥ proktaḥ śūnyakaḥ tu yathā sthitaḥ pūrakaḥ pūraṇāt vāyoḥ tad nirodhāt ca kumbhakaḥ dehinaḥ dakṣiṇe bhāge piṅgalā nāḍikā ramṛtā dakṣiṇetara gā yā ca iḍā sā nāḍikā smṛtā daivatam tatas śūnyam nirālambam madhye sva ātmani yojayet vāhya sthāt bodhanāt vāyoḥ śūnyaka tvam vinirdiśet āpyāyanam bhavet tena plāvanam kalmaṣasya tu aṅguṣṭha agrāt samārabhya brahmarandhreṇa mocayet saṃkocya kucikā cakram ūrdhvam nītvā rasā trayam saṃkṣobhya śaṅkhinīm samyak tatas brahmaguhām nayet anena śodhayet mārgam aiśvaram vimalam muniḥ sumukṣūṇām sadā vatsaiḥ yoga aṅgam yoga siddhaye tu aṅgulyāḥ tu śanais śanais saumyena ākarṣayet vāyum nābhau ākṛṣya dhārayet jāyate vatsarāt yogī jarā maraṇa varjitaḥ vāyum ākarṣayet vāhyam vāmayā ca udaram bharet nābhi nāsā antarā dhyāyan tris prāṇān ca jayet dhruvam triṣu sthāneṣu dhāraṇāt aṅguṣṭha nābhi nāsā agre vāyum yogī jita āsanaḥ apānam kaṭi deśe tu pṛṣṭhatas vai vinirdiśet nirālambe manaḥ kṛtvā kṣaṇāt prāṇa jitaḥ bhavet indriyāṇām vicaratām viṣayeṣu svabhāvāt pañcānām pañcama ādya itara ejane udvātān daśa pañca eva kārayet dhāraṇām budhaḥ prāṇa vāyum nivāya eva manaḥ sūrye antare kṣipet devān ca siddhān gandharva aśva araṇān khecarān gaṇān māsa abhyāsa yogena sūkṣma jyotiḥ prapaśyati dṛṣṭe na syāt jarā mṛtyuḥ sarvajñaḥ ca prajāyate sphoṭa ākhyā nāḍikā proktā kūrma lokaḥ tadā antare bhūtam bhavyam bhaviṣyam ca vartamānam ca dūratas yat tat bhavet nūnam sphoṭa ākhye jñānam abhyaset lalāṭe mūrdhani hṛdaye sadāśivam anusmaret dhyātvā evam ātmani vibhum dhyānam tat sūrayaḥ viduḥ na jighrati na spṛśati na kiṃcid vā samīkṣate guhya udara ādi sthāneṣu vāyum nāsām vicintayet īśaḥ aham iti yogi indraḥ para ānanda eka vigrahaḥ ekāntara unmanībhāvaḥ samādhiḥ abhidhīyate na sthūlam na kṛśam vā api na hrasvam na api lopitam na śuklam na api vā pītam na kṛṣṇam na api karburram hṛd padma nilaye viśva ākhyam viśva sambhavam parastāt tam asaṃsthitam pradhāna puruṣa atītam ākāśam daharam śivam tad antar sarva bhūtānām īśvaram brahma rūpiṇam dhyāyet anādi madhya antam ānanda ādi guṇa ālayam mahantam puruṣam brahma brahmānam brahma ca avyayam oṃkāra ante oṃkāra ante saṃsthāpya paramātmani prākāśe devam īśānam dhyāyīta ākāśa madhya gam yat kāraṇam sarva bhāvānām ānanda eka rasa āśrayam purāṇam puruṣam śambhum dhyāyet mucyeta bandhanāt mūḍhaḥ yathā śva lāṅgalaiḥ samudram tartum icchati tathā vinā śambhu sevām saṃsāra taraṇam na hi mumukṣavaḥ pātum tiṣṭhet maheśena saḥ aśnute yogam aiśvaram na ekalakṣam dvilakṣam vā tri lakṣam na mava ātmakam saṃsthāpya mayi ca ātmānam param jyotiṣi nirguṇe tiṣṭhataḥ sākṣātasya ca anubhavaḥ bhavet sarva jñaḥ paripūrṇaḥ ca jarā maraṇa varjitaḥ mad prasādāt bhavet yogī na anyathā krauñcasūdanaiḥ mām ekam śaraṇam gacchet ajñānam nāśayāmi aham brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāḥ vaiśyāḥ śūdrāḥ ca anye ca saṃkarāḥ mad bhakti bhāvanā pūtāḥ yānti mad paramam padam yoginām karmiṇām ca eva tāpasānām yata ātmanām mama eva gatiḥ teṣām na anyat asti iti niśvayaḥ iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure śivara kanda saṃvāde yamaniyamaprāṇāyāmādikathanam nāma dvādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ bhūta kāryayā idam deham āpat roga ākulam param mad sukha duḥkha ātmakaiḥ sadā abhibhūtaḥ yadā yogī duḥkhaiḥ adhyātma saṃbhavaiḥ yātanāya upasargāṇām prasādāt yoginām vada maheśvaraḥ uvāca sāttvikāḥ rājasāḥ vighnāḥ tāmasāḥ tu iha yoginām prātibhā śravaṇa a vārttā darśana āsvāda vedanāḥ daridraḥ aham aham ca āḍhyaḥ śūraḥ aham durbalaḥ tathā mūrkhaḥ aham ca su vidvāḥ ca surūpaḥ aham arūpavān dātā aham kṛpaṇaḥ ca aham sukhī bhogī aham eva ca akulīnaḥ kulīnaḥ ca kaṇṭakaḥ kaṇṭaka ujjhitaḥ ahaṃkāra mayam kiṃcid yat tat kṛtsnam hi rājasam andha tvam ca eva bādhirya paṅga tvam duṣṭa roga tā śiras rogaḥ jvaraḥ śūla aiyakṣma mūrchā bhrama ādayaḥ rājasāḥ tāmasāḥ sarve tamas uhaṃkāra saṃyutāḥ vyādhayaḥ miśra bhāvena pīḍayanti iha dehinam kevalam jāḍya bhāvena mūḍha tvam mohanaiḥ tathā ajñāna tvam ca mūka tvam ityādyāḥ tāmasāḥ smṛtāḥ yātudhānāḥ ca kiṃnara uraga rākṣasāḥ tad deva dānavaiḥ raudrāḥ ca daityāḥ mātar ajāḥ gaṇāḥ tāmasāḥ tu grahāḥ bhūtāḥ vāyu bhūtāḥ naram sadā pīḍayanti iha vighnāḥ hi yoga abhyāsa ratam grahaiḥ evamādi upasargāṇām vāraṇāya ca dhāraṇām vakṣyāmi vividhām vatsa yoginām siddhi hetave tvac ādi sapta dhātūnām ekībhūtam vicintayet praṇavam kaṇṭha nāsā agre sa bījam vahni dīpitam pitta roga abhibhūtaḥ vā yogī yoga parāyaṇaḥ praviśya brahma rūpeṇa dehaiḥ nirvāṇa jam smaret yathā nāśayet andha tām yogī divya dṛṣṭiḥ prajan pītvā pārthivataśvena su ambham vāyoḥ vināśayet puṣṭiḥ eva atulā tasya sthira svam rujā hīna tā śrotram ākāśa vāyuvoḥ ca atra ekatvam vicintayet śṛṇoti dūratas sarva śruta ghārī bhavet sadā saroja rasanāyām ca tad draṣṭāram sa karṇikam prajñā ca evam smṛtiḥ medhā kavi tvam buddhiḥ uttamā stambhanam duṣṭa tvānām sarva vāyūn jayet sadā hṛd saroja gatam devam aṣṭādaśa bhujaiḥ yutam nīla aruṇam mahā kārya kcindra jaṭā dharam siṃha carma ambaram bhīmam sarva ābharaṇa bhūṣitam bhujaṃgam hāra ābharaṇam sarva kaṅka nūpuram bhā bhāsita digānanam nāśay andha tā ityādi śloka pūrvam kama śata eva pustaka śloka artha idam dṛś manena utyāpayet kṣaṇāt lakṣam ādhāya tatra eva yojayet māye ṣaṇmukhaiḥ ghṛtam ghṛteṣu eva niyuktam prayāti ca aikyāt aviśeṣa bhāvam <extra id iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure śiva skanda saṃvāde sāttvikarājasavighnādikathanam nāma trayodaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca saṃpravakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvam muni puṃgavāḥ tatra kṛṣṇāṣṭamī puṇyā sarva pāpa praṇāśanā pustakeṣu yad ekādaśa adhyāyaḥ tad eva atra saṃgrah tat tat tat vibhūti dam tat tat kṛṣṇāṣṭamī tratam kṛtvā brahmā brahmatvam āpnuyāt candraḥ candra tvam āpannaḥ gaṇeśa tvam gaṇādhipaḥ senāpati tvam ca tathā ca anye gaṇeśvarāḥ kṛtvā ca aiśvaryam āpannāḥ saubhāgyam deva vallabhāḥ vratasya asya prabhāvena lakṣmyāḥ patiḥ abhūt hariḥ yayātiḥ sārvabhauma tvam tathā ca anye nṛpa uttamāḥ munayaḥ siddhāḥ gandharvāṇām ca kanyakāḥ muni puṃgavāḥ kṛtvā ca eva parām siddhim prāptāḥ ca muni puṃgavāḥ nandīśvareṇa yat proktam nāradāya mahātmane kṛṣṇāṣṭamīvratam śreṣṭham sarva kāma phala pradam meroḥ yat akṣiṇam śṛṅgam sura asura namaskṛtam tatra nandīśvaram dṛṣṭvā sarvajñam śambhu vallabham upāsyamānam munibhiḥ stūyamānam marut gaṇaiḥ abravīt praṇipatya atha daṇḍa vat nāradaḥ muniḥ nāradaḥ uvāca saubhāgyam kāntim aiśvaryam apatyam ca yaśaḥ tathā muktimante ca paśu pāśa vimocanīm bhagavant tat vratam brūhi kāruṇyāt śaṃkara bhiyam bhavati kṛṣṇa aṣṭamī vratam śreṣṭham asti devaṛṣe śṛṇu gaṇeśa tvam mayā labdham yena cīrṇena nāradaiḥ māse mārgaśire prāpte kṛṣṇa aṣṭamyām jita indriyaḥ aśvattha dantakāṣṭhena kṛtvā vai dantadhāvanam snānam kṛtvā ca vidhivat tarpaṇam ca eva nāradaiḥ mad bhavanam paścāt pūjayet śaṃkaram prabhum prāśya vidhivat bhavet atirātrasya yajñasya phalam aṣṭaguṇam bhavet pūjayet śam bhu nāmānam bhagavantam maheśvaram vājapeya aṣṭaka phalam prāpnoti śraddhayā anvitaḥ māghe vaṭasya kathitam go kṣīram prāśanam smṛtam māheśvaram su saṃpūjya gomedhasya aṣṭakam phalam ca tat eva uktam kāryam vai prāśanam ca tat saṃpūjayet mahādevam rājasūya aṣṭakam phalam kāṣṭham audumbaram caitre prāśane varjitāḥ janāḥ pūjayet sthāṇu nāmānam aśvamedha phalam labhet mahat saṃpūjya vaiśākhe pītvā ca eva kuśa udakam prāpnoti eva hi nāradaiḥ jyeṣṭhe lākṣam bhavet kāṣṭham pūjyaḥ paśupatiḥ vibhuḥ gavām śṛṅgodakam prāśya svapet evasya saṃnidhau avāpnuyāt māsāḍhe ca ugranāmānam iṣṭvā prāśya ca gomayam tu yajñasya phalam aṣṭaguṇam bhavet pālāśam śrāvaṇe proktam saṃpūjya nāradaiḥ prāśayitvā arka pattrāṇi kalpam śiva pure vaset māse bhādrapade aṣṭamyām tryambakam saṃprapūjayet mās aśanam bilva pattrasya sarva dīkṣā phalam bhavet madhu vṛkṣasya dantakāṣṭham udīritam pūjayet bhaktyā prāśayet taṇḍula udakam pauṇḍarīkasya yajñasya phalam aṣṭaguṇam labhet māse tu kārttike aṣṭamyām īśāna ākhyam prapūjayet pañcagavyam sakṛt pītvā agniṣṭoma phalam labhet varṣa ante bhojayet viprāḥ śiva bhakti parāyaṇān mahatyā hiraṇyam vāsāṃsi bhaktyā tebhyaḥ nivedayet sa ratnām tāmra kalaśīm gām alaṃkṛtya nārada alaṃkāram ca vastram ca dakṣiṇām ca sva śaktitas yat kalpa koṭi śatam sāgram śiva loke mahīyate taḥ uvāca evam nandīśvarāt śrutvā nāradaḥ muni puṃgavāḥ tat tat tat tat yayau badarikāśramam yaḥ paṭhet vā śṛṇuyāt api nāma caturdaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ taḥ uvāca yat uktam bhānunā pūrva yājñavalkyāya yogine uvāca jayā ca vijayā ca eva kiṃphalā kiparāyaṇā tasyām viśiṣṭam yat puṇyam vada kaśyapa nandana dvādaśī viṣṇu dayitā dvādaśī vaiṣṇavī tithiḥ ṛuklapakṣe dvijaśreṣṭhaiḥ vijayā sā prakīrtitā upoṣyā sā prayatnena sarva pāpa praṇāśanā yā tu puṣyeṇa saṃyuktā phālgunasya sitā tu vai sā jayā dvādaśī nāma sarva pāpa kṣayaṃkarā tasyām snātaḥ sadā snātaḥ bhavet vai na atra saṃśayaḥ saṃpūjya vastra puṣpa ādyaiḥ phalam sāyam samaśnute adhīte śraddhā samanvitaḥ sapta janma kṛtam pāpam su alpam vā yadi vā bahu tasyām snātaḥ dvijottamaiḥ yaḥ kṛtvā dvādaśīm imām kṣapayet bhaktimān naraḥ ekādaśyām nirāhāraḥ dvādaśyām viṣṇum arcayet pādau prathamam kūrmāya ca tathā kaṭim iti iti vai iti ca pratyeka nāmnā ca netre dve buddha nāmnā tathā śiraḥ bhaktyā ca āssrādhya govindam gopālam ca tathā niśi tatas tasya agratas śuddham nyaset kṛṣṇājinam budhaḥ tasya upari tilānām tu kṛṣṇānām āḍhakam nyaset tila alābhe yavāḥ kāryāḥ godhūma āra tad alābhāt raupyam tāmram vā pātram kuryāt sva śaktitas pracchādya pātram vāsobhiḥ ahataiḥ su parīkṣitaiḥ sauvarṇa vāmanam kṛtvā sa akṣasūtra kamaṇḍalum yathāśaktyā kṛtam haravam kṛta yajña upavītinam evaṃrūpam tu tam kṛtvā vāmanam bhaktimān naraḥ matsyaḥ kūrmaḥ varāhaḥ ca nārasiṃhaḥ atha vāmanaḥ rāmaḥ rāmaḥ ca kṛṣṇaḥ ca buddhaḥ kalkī ca te daśa bhaktasya atra viśeṣeṇa phalam koṭi guṇa uttaram chattram ca eva akṣasūtram ca pāduke guḍikām tathā jāgaram tatra kurvīta gīta vādi nāditaiḥ pradeyam śāstra vidvase brāhmaṇāya kuṭumbine veda adhyetre samam dānam dviguṇam tad vide tathā mahā ācārye dānam ekam ca sahastra guṇitam tathā evam dattvā vidhānena brāhmaṇāya ca bhaktyāḥ mantreṇa anena dātavyam purāṇa paṭhitena ca mantreṇa pratigṛhṇīyāt brāhmaṇaḥ ca dvijottamaiḥ vāmanaḥ pratigṛhṇāti vāmanaḥ vai dadāti ca annam prajāpatiḥ viṣṇu rudra indra śaśi bhāskarāḥ parjanyaḥ varuṇaḥ sūryaḥ salilam keśavaḥ śivaḥ su aṣṭā yamaḥ vaiśravaṇaḥ pāpam haratu mama sadā bhojanam dattvā yathāśakti atha dakṣiṇām pṛṣadājyam ca saṃprāśya paścāt bhuñjīta vāgyataḥ bhūyas yathā icchayā rātrau sarvatra eṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ brahma loka ādi lokeṣu bhuktvā bhogān anekaśas punar svargāt bhuvam prāpya jāyate mahatām kule saptadvīpā ādhipatyam ca prāpnuyāt na atra saṃśayaḥ iti idam śṛṇuyāt nityam anuttamam sarva nāma taḥ uvāca anyat vratam idam vakṣye śṛṇudhvam muni puṃgavāḥ saubhāgya vardhanam puṇyam mahāpātaka nāśanam sarva duṣṭa upaśamanam sarva aiśvarya madam śivam yam yam kāmayate kāmam tam tam prāpnoti mānavaḥ purā devena rudreṇa dagdhaḥ kāmaḥ durāsadaḥ upoṣitā tithiḥ tena tena anaṅgatrayodaśī śukla pakṣe trayodaśyām māsi mārgaśire dvijāḥ snānam kṛtvā atha vidhinā sa upavāsaḥ jita indriyaḥ tila hoṃmam kuryāt aṣṭa uttaram śatam tat tat tat tat tat svapet niśi ha daśānām aśvamedhānām phalam prāpnoti mānavaḥ yogeśvaram su saṃpūjya pauṣe candanam rājasūyasya yajñasya phailam ānoti mānavaḥ nāṭeśvaram su saṃpūjya māgha māse jita indriyaḥ mauktikam prāśya vipra indrāḥ phalam tasya vadāmi aham saṃpūjya phālgune vīram kadanelam prāśayaḥ nārī ca ca prapūjayet yat jātīphalam ca saṃprāśya go sahasra phalam labhet prāśayet umābhartā iti nāmānam āṣāḍhe saṃprapūjayet tila udakam tu saṃprāśya puṇḍarīka phalam labhet pūjayet śrāvaṇe śūlapāṇinam parameśvaram māse bhādrapade vimāḥ sadyojātam prapūjayet agarum prāśayitvā tu sarva yajña phalam labhet māse ca āśvayuje prāpte tridaśādhipatim yajet svarṇa udakam tu saṃprāśya svarṇa koṭi phalam labhet pūjayet pratimāsam pravakṣyāmi dantakāṣṭhāni vai dvijāḥ mallikā khādiram ca eva lakṣa apāmārga jam tathā mālatī vaṭa jam tathā mālatyāḥ prathamam tāvat tatas marutrakam tathā tathā kundam arka pattrāṇi suvratāḥ tatas mandāra puṣpāṇi mallikā kusumāni ca bhādambam yūthikāpuṣpam dhattūram śatapattrakam durvā aṅkurāṇi deyāni naivedyāni yathākramam madhu odanam kṛsaram śarkarā āmodakāḥ tathā kaṃsāram yāvakāḥ tatra tatas sauhālikā bhavet pañcakhādyam param proktam ghṛtapūram anantaram nānā vidhānam naivedyam kārttikyām parikalpayet pūjā nāmāni vakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvam muni puṃgavāḥ śaṃkarāya namaḥ pādau gauye gulphe śivāya ca hi śivāyai jānunī pūjya śaṃbhavāya udbhavāya ca kaiṭim manmatha nāśāya madanāyai surerśvare bhavāya saṃpūjya bhavānyai namaḥ iti umām deva adhidevāya aparṇāyai namaḥ śivām bhīma ugra rūpāya girijāyai namaḥ śivām skandham tridaśa vandyāya triśūlinyai namaḥ śivām bāhū dhūrjaya iti uktvā dhūsarāyai namaḥ śivām hastau śūladharāya iti śūlinyai namaḥ iti umām mukham devasya saṃpūjya vāmadeva iti vāstaḥ vāmāyai namaḥ iti uktvā nāsām ca eva kapāline mṛḍānyai namaḥ iti uktvā lalāṭam ca indu dhāriṇe alakāyai namaḥ paścāt trinetrāya namaḥ tathā tryakṣyai saṃpūjayet devīm śiraḥ gaṅgādharāya ca tatas pūjya vyomakeśāya vai namaḥ keśān saṃpūjya vidhivat keśinyai ca namaḥ namaḥ śukla vastreṇa saṃchādya saṃpūjya vidhivat vijāḥ mad atha tam dadyāt vitta śāyya vivarjitaḥ kalaśāḥ sa udakāḥ deyāḥ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ sa dakṣiṇāḥ brāhmaṇān bhojayet bhaktyā śiva bhakti parāyaṇān evam karoti yaḥ viprāḥ bhaktyā anaṅgatrayodaśīm prāpnoti rājyam saubhāgyam putrān ca cira jīvinaḥ mahā lokam ca saṃprāpya śambhoḥ priyatamaḥ bhavet nāma ṣoḍaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ yat uktam bhavatā sūta naiṣkalam jñānam uttamam hṛṣitam ca akhilam asmābhiḥ manāṃsi hṛṣitāni naḥ bhaktiḥ ca śāśvate śambhau jātā naḥ hi śāśvatā brūhi taḥ uvāca caturṇām api varṇānām vidhim vakṣyāmi suvratāḥ yat uktam bhānunā pūrve manave parameṣṭhine yena viśveśvaraḥ śambhuḥ karma yoga rataiḥ sadā na ca anyena iti eṣā vaidikā śrutiḥ brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ śūdraḥ ucyate yad yad yad yad yad tad tad trayaḥ ādyāḥ dvijāḥ smṛtāḥ pañcamaḥ na upapadyate sarveṣām āśramāṇām ca vihitam daṇḍadhāraṇam na daṇḍena vinā kaśvid āśramī iti nigadyate brahmacārī bhavet daṇḍī kṛṣṇa ajina dharaiḥ tathā mekhalī ca tathā muṇḍī śikhī vā yadi vā jaṭī bhikṣā āhāreṇa satatam vartanam tasya suvratāḥ tathā kuryāt sāyam prātar yathāvidhi snātvā saṃtarpya deva ādīn devatā abhyarcanam tatas abhivādana śīlaḥ syāt vṛddheṣu ca yathākramam hi ādhyātmikam vaidikam vā tathā laukikam eva vā ādadīta guroḥ yasmāt tam pūrvam abhivādayet asau aham iti brūyāt pratyutthāya yavīyasaḥ na abhivāyāḥ tu vipreṇa kṣatriya ādyāḥ kathaṃcana mā bhikṣām āhṛ suvrataḥ nivedya gurave aśrīyāt vāgyataḥ tad anujñayā bhaikṣeṇa vartanam nityam na eka anna ādī vratī bhavet upavāsa samā bhikṣā proktā vai brahmacāriṇām prāc mukhaḥ anna ādi bhuñjīta sūrya abhimukhaḥ eva vā na ābāda daṅmukhaḥ nityam vidhiḥ eṣa sanātanaḥ bhuñjīta maunī satatam smaret evam sadāśivam sa upānatkaḥ jala sthaḥ vā na uṣṇīṣī ca ācamet budhaḥ prāśnīya atris apaḥ pūrvam brāhmaṇaiḥ prayataḥ dvijaḥ saṃvṛttā mūlena mukham ca evam upaspṛśet aṅguṣṭha anāmikābhyām ca saṃspṛśet nayana dvayam aṅguṣṭha tarjanībhyām ca saṃspṛśena asikā puṭe tad kaniṣṭhā aṅguṣṭha yogena spṛśet śratra yugam dvijaḥ sarvābhiḥ aṅgulibhiḥ ca hṛdayam ca talena vā saṃspṛśet vai śiraḥ tadvat aṅguṣṭhena athavā dvayam divā mūtra purīṣe ca śarvaryāḥ dakṣiṇā mukhaḥ ācchādya parṇaiḥ vasudhām tṛṇaiḥ vā mauna saṃyutaḥ śiraḥ prāhṛtya vipra indrāḥ na anyathā ca kadācana pathi goṣṭhe nadī tīre chāyāyām kūpa saṃnidhau tuṣa aṅgāra kapāleṣu na kṣetre na catuṣpathe na udyāne na śmaśāne ca na paśyan tārakā ādikān na ca eva abhimukhaḥ strīṇām guru brāhmaṇayoḥ gavām maucam paścāt prakurvīta gandha lepa kṣaya avadhi manasaḥ śuddhiḥ yathā bhavati tat vijāḥ ji indriya syāt satatam vaśya ātman akrodhana śuci prayuñjīta sadā vācam madhurām hita bhāṣiṇīm dyūtam jana parīvādam strī velā ālambhanam tathā paryuṣitam varṇya kṛtam ca lavaṇam tathā mala apakarṣaṇam snānam śūdra ādyaiḥ abhibhāṣaṇam vivarjayet uda kumbham sumanasaḥ go śakṛt mṛttikī kuśān ācamya saṃyataḥ nityam adhīyīta chudak mukhaḥ upasaṃgṛhya tad pādau vīkṣamāṇaḥ guroḥ mukham sarveṣām eva bhūtānām vedaḥ cakṣuḥ sanātanam vedaḥ śreyaskaraḥ puṃsām na anyaḥ iti abravīt raviḥ an adhītya dvijaḥ yaḥ tu śāstrāṇi su bahūni api mā asau narakāṇi prapadyate na asscāra phalam āpnoti yathā śūdraḥ tathā eva saḥ śūdra putraḥ sa vijñeyām na veda phalam aśrute vedam vedau tathā veda vedān ca caturaḥ dvijāḥ adhītya gurave dattvā dakṣiṇām ca bhavet gṛhī rūpa lakṣaṇa saṃyuktām kanyām uddāhayet tatas amātṛ gotra prabhavām asamāna ārṣa gotra jām mātuḥ pañcamāt ūrdhvam pituḥ saptamāt tathā roga hīnām surūpiṇīm mātuḥ pañcamāt avapituḥ saptamāt tathā dhārayet vaiṇavām yaṣṭim antarvāsaḥ tathā uttaram yajñopavīta dvitayam sa udakam ca kamaṇḍalum chattram ca uṣṇīpam amalam pāduke vā api upānahau raukme ca kuṇḍale nityam kṛtta keśa nakhaḥ śuciḥ paṣṭa ṣṭamyau pañcadaśīm amāvāsyām caturdaśīm brahmacārī bhavet nityam janma ca viśeṣataḥ mādadīta āvasathya agnim juhuyāt jātavedasam akurvāṇaḥ patati āśu nirayān ati bhīṣaṇān kuryāt rahmāṇi karmāṇi saṃdhyā upāsanam eva ca vaiṣavān buddhi sādṛśyam ācaran vicaret sadā tam ācāram niṣeveta sādhūn vakṣyāmi sāṃpratam yaḥ taiḥ anuṣṭhitaḥ dharmaḥ śruti smṛtyā saṃgataḥ sat ācāraḥ saḥ vai proktaḥ devadevena śambhunā kurukṣetrāḥ ca matsya arthe pāñcālāḥ śūrasena jāḥ ete deśāḥ puṇya deśāḥ sarve ca anye ca ninditāḥ deśepaveṣu nivaset rāhmaṇaiḥ dharma kāṅkṣibhiḥ aṅga vaṅga kaliṅgān ca saurāṣṭram gurjaram tathā ābhīram kauḍūṇam ca eva drāviḍam dakṣiṇāpatham ca māgadham ca eva deśān etān ca varjayet nityam svādhyāya śīlaḥ syāt pañcayajña parāyaṇaḥ sāvitrī jāpya nirataḥ śiva bhakti parāyaṇaḥ śrāddha kṛt dāna nirataḥ kṣamā yuktaḥ dayālukaḥ gṛhasthaḥ tu samākhyātaḥ na gṛheṇa gṛhī bhavet na śarīram vinā devaḥ pūjyate girijāpatiḥ brahmacārī gṛhasthaḥ vā vānaprasthaḥ athavā yatiḥ iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde varṇa āśrama ācāra vidhi kathanam saptadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ taḥ uvāca bhid na hiṃsyāt sarva bhūtāni na vedānām ca kutsanam nindakānām maheśasya śuddhiḥ na khalu dṛśyate jalam tṛṇam vā śākam vā mṛdam vā kāṣṭham eva vā prāṇān apaharati eṣa yācakaḥ tasya durmatiḥ grahītavyāni puṣpāṇi deva arcana vidhau dvijaiḥ tṛṇam kāṣṭham phalam puṣpam prakāśam vai haret budhaḥ tila mudrā yava ādīnām muṣṭiḥ yā ādyā yadi sthitaiḥ anṛtāt pāradāryāt ca tathā abhakṣyasya bhakṣaṇāt pūrvaḥ pūrvaḥ abhivādyaḥ syāt pūrva abhāve paraḥ paraḥ tripuṇḍra dhārī satatam brāhmaṇaḥ sarva karmasu na mūkhaiḥ saha saṃvāsaḥ patitaiḥ na kadācana paiśunyam śuṣka vairāṇi vivādam varjayet sadā hayatīm gām para kṣetre na ca ācakṣīta kasyacid tithim pakṣasya na brūyāt nakṣatrāṇi na nirdiśet na pāpam pāpinām brūyāt tathā apāpam apāpinām yāni mithyā abhiśastānām patanti aśrṛṇi rodanāt tāni putrān paśūn ghnanti teṣām mithyā abhiśaṃsinām brahmahatyā surā pānam steyam guru aṅga anna āgamaḥ dṛṣṭam virodhanam vṛddhaiḥ nārita midhyā abhiśaṃsini mānam madam tathā śokam dveṣam ca parivarjayet ravivāre na kurvīta bhṛṣṭa bhairava bhakṣaṇam dhana kāmaḥ janaḥ satyam na atra kāryā vicāraṇā na kuryāt kasyacid pīḍām sutam śiṣyam ca tāḍayet na nadīṣu nadīm brūyāt parvateṣu ca parvatam śiraḥ abhyaṅga avaśiṣṭena tailena aṅgam na lepayet sarpa śastraiḥ krīḍeta svāni khāni na saṃspṛśet na saṃhatābhyām pāṇibhyām kaṇḍūyet ātmanaḥ śiraḥ devān kīrtaye dṛṣīn viśveśvaram umākāntam viśva antaryāmiṇam vibhum na brahma ādyaiḥ samam brūyāt śaktibhiḥ na ca pārvatīm brūyāt yadi samam śambhum brahma viṣṇu ādibhiḥ suraiḥ yaḥ kaścid tamasā āviṣṭaḥ kadācid na eva tam spṛśet tathā devīm ca girijām dvijaiḥ śreyas arthibhiḥ sadā para striyam na bhāṣeta na ayājyam yājayet vijāḥ na na guroḥ chāyām na guroḥ sadā kuryāt bhūmim vyāhṛtibhiḥ spṛṣṭrā khanamānam ca āśayā uddhṛtā asi iti saṃgṛhya gandha dvāra iti gomayam apa agham iti apāmārgaiḥ dūrvā saṃgṛhya durvayā hi jala tīram samāsādya śucau deśe samāhitaḥ ādityāḥ iti saṃprokṣya kūlam tīrthasya suvrataḥ hi śucau deśe pratiṣṭhāpya gāyatryā prokṣayet tatas bhāga dvayam sa tām paścāt ekam dikṣu visarjayet tad avaśiṣṭena bhāgena mantraiḥ vā ālepayet kramāt akṣībhyām iti mantreṇa mukham ālepayet budhaḥ tathā grīvābhyām iti ca grīvām tathā bhujau śarīram yajñam uktvā atha x hṛdayam parilepayet vinikṣipet mūrdhānam iti mantreṇa tila dūrvā akṣata ādikam hiraṇyaśṛṅgam iti uktvā tīrtham saṃprārthya buddhimān japet śuddha matiḥ paścāt sūktam ca eva aghamarṣaṇam dvipadām ca japet devīm sarva pāpa praṇāśanām idam tu vāruṇam snānam mantra snānam atha ucyate tu āgneyam bhasmanā snānam vāyavyam rajasā mavām mānasam snānam uttamam traivarṇikānām sarveṣām gāyatrī paramā gatiḥ yat gāyatryāḥ param tattvam devadevaḥ maheśvaraḥ iti jñātvā japet vidvāḥ gāyatryāḥ phalam aśnute yaḥ hi anyathā tu manute gāyatrī śiva rūpiṇīm pādāḥ catvāraḥ gāyatryāḥ vedāḥ catvāraḥ eva te māt viraści viṣṇuḥ deśāḥ pādānām devatāḥ kramāt evam jñātvā vidhānena gāyatrī vedamātrīm japet māheśvaram jyotiḥ nityam eva prakāśate upatiṣṭhet atha ādityam rudra rūpiṇam avyayam pāvamānāni sūktāni brahmayajña prasiddhaye japet samāhitaḥ bhūtvā rudrān ca eva viśeṣataḥ xc ṣaṣ akṣareṇa mantreṇa māna stokyā tathā eva ca na asti iti uvāca bhagavān devadevaḥ svayam raviḥ na a saṃpūjya mahādevam bhuñjīta brāhmaṇaḥ sadā brāhmaṇa kṣatriya viśām karmiṇām yoginām api mahāyajñān gṛhasthaḥ śraddhayā anvitaḥ pañcayajña parityāgāt āśramaḥ uṃdavahīyate deva yajñaḥ bhūta yajñaḥ pitṛ yajñaḥ tathā aparaḥ mānuṣaḥ brahmayajñaḥ ca pañca yajñāḥ prakīrtitāḥ huta śeṣeṇa bhūtebhyaḥ bālam bhūta makham viduḥ nitya śrāddham tad ṛddhim pitṛ yajñam pracakṣate yathāśakti annum udṛtya padadyāt rāhmaṇāya vai pūjayet bhaktyā śiva bhāva samanvitaḥ madadyāt vratakāram vā bhikṣām ca bhava bhāvataḥ etān kṛtvā eva satatam bhuñjīta āśrama dharmabhiḥ anyathā yaḥ hi bhuṅkte annam pretya śūkaratām vrajet yadi viśveśvare sthāṇī bhaktiḥ ekā eva niścalā taḥ uvāca śrāddham darśe atha kartavyam aṣṭakāsu ayana dvaye viṣuve ca vyatīpāte tīrtheṣu ca viśeṣataḥ parīkṣya brāhmaṇān samyak veda vedāṅga pāragān ca tad abhāve śiva bhaktānām sat ācāra ratān dvijān bhojayet śraddhayā śrāddhe śiva buddhayā samāhitaḥ niratāḥ somapāḥ saṃyata indriyāḥ agnihotra parāḥ śāntāḥ vahcāḥ guru pūjakāḥ triṇāciketāḥ śiṣyāḥ ca trimadhu trisuparṇikāḥ mantra brāhmaṇa vettāraḥ adhyātma śāstra niratāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ paṅkti pāvanāḥ ekam vā bhojayet vimam śiva bhakti parāyaṇam tena pūtāḥ bhavanti eva ye kecid paṅkti dūṣakāḥ badha bandha upajīvī ca vṛṣalaḥ śūdra yojakāḥ veda vikrayiṇaḥ ca anye kopinaḥ kuṇḍa golakau yasthāḥ lamba karṇāḥ ca nityam rāja upasevakāḥ bhiṣaj śāstra upajīvinaḥ vyādhinaḥ kāvya kartāraḥ gāyakāḥ ca eva gotriṇaḥ yad nindā ratāḥ ca eva kṛtaghnāḥ piśunāḥ tathā hīna atirikta dehāḥ ca śrāddhe varjyāḥ prayatnāt adhvānam kalaham krodham putra bhāryā ādi tāḍanam prakṣālayet tatas pādau arcite maṇḍale śubhe vartulam caitra vaiśyasya śūdrasya abhyukṣaṇam smṛtam paścāt śrāddhasya rakṣā artham tilān ca vikiret tatas te te tad tad tad iti ṛcā mad naḥ devyāḥ jalam kṣiptvā sa pavitre tu bhājane yavān yavaḥ asi iti tathā gandha puṣpam ca nikṣipet madadyāt gandha mālya ādi dhūpam vāsāṃsi śaktitas apasavyam tatas kṛtvā pitṛn āvāhayet tatas uśantaḥ tu ati ca ṛcā āvāhya tad anujñayā yapet āyantu naḥ ṛcam tilaḥ asi iti nilān tathā pitṛbhyaḥ sthānam asi iti tatas anaukaraṇam matam mahādevasya puratas goṣṭhe vā śraddhayā anvitaḥ brāhmaṇān ca eva bhojayet mahā pāyasam dadyāt bhakṣyāṇi su bahūni api lehyam coṣyam tathā kāmapuṣpam eva phalam vinā api dattāni api niṣiddhāni śrāddham na eva akṣayam bhavet na aśnāti yaḥ dvijaḥ māṃsam niyuktaḥ pitṛ karmaṇi dharma śāstram purāṇam ca tathā atharvaśiraḥ tathā rudrān ca pauruṣam sūktam brāhmaṇān śrāvayet tatas bhuñjīran brāhmaṇāḥ sarve vāgyatāḥ ghṛta bhojanāḥ vikiram nikṣipet paścāt śeṣam annam atha abravīt dāt vai dakṣiṇām śaktyā svadhākāram udīrayet dātāraḥ naḥ abhivardhantām vājevāja iti vai ṛcam bhoktā ca śrāddha dara tasyām rajanyām maithunam tyajet adhvagaḥ vyasanī ca eva viśeṣeṇa ha anagnikaḥ māmaśrāddham dvijaḥ kuryāt sadā eva hi śraddhayā tu kṛte śrāddhe bhagavant nīlalohitaḥ taḥ uvāca atha dharmaḥ vanasthānām ucyate śṛṇuta dvijāḥ śarīram ātmanaḥ dṛṣṭvā palita ayaiḥ ca dūṣitam phala mūla aśanaḥ nityam pañcayajña parāyaṇaḥ tithim pūjayet bhaktyā matvā śarvaḥ iti śrutiḥ aṣṭau grāsān ca bhuñjīta cīra vāsāḥ bhavet jaṭī bhavet triṣavaṇaḥ trāyī nityam svādhyāya tatparaḥ dayām ca sarva bhūteṣu na kuryāt niśi bhojanam varjayet grāma jātāni puṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca yadi gacchet vanī bhāryā prāyaścittī bhavet vijaḥ madhya garbhaḥ bhavet tasyāḥ sa cāṇḍāla samaḥ bhavet sarva bhūta anukampī syāt saṃvibhāna rataḥ sadā parivādam mṛpāvādam nidrā ālasyam vivarjayet śīrṇa parṇa aśanaḥ vā syāt kṛcchra vartayet sadā śiva pūjā rataḥ nityam śiva dhyāna parāyaṇaḥ parām gatim avāpnoti dehānte śāśvatam padam vedānta abhyāsa nirataḥ dāntaḥ śāntaḥ jita indriyaḥ jīrṇa kaupīna vāsāḥ syāt muṇḍaḥ nagnaḥ athavā bhavet tridaṇḍī vā bhavet vidvāḥ iti eṣā vaidikā śrutiḥ samaḥ śatrau ca mitre ca tathā māna apamānayoḥ eka anna ādī bhavet yaḥ tu kadācid lampaṭaḥ yatiḥ niṣkṛtinā eva tasya asti dharma śāstreṣu sarvathā bhavet triṣavaṇa snāyī bhasma uddhūlita vigrahaḥ anantam nirguṇam śāntam puruṣam prakṛtyāḥ param tat sarva jagantām ādhāram sarvatomukham cit rūpam śaṃkareṃ sthāṇum ānandam ajaram vibhum jñānī mokṣam avāpnoti virāṭpada makhe rataḥ iti sarvam aśeṣeṇa cāturāśramyam īritam śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde vānaprasthādidharmakathanam nāma viṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ manvantarāṇi teṣām ca caritam tathā pratisargaḥ punar ca eva yathā bhavati kṛtstra aṃśaḥ brūhi naḥ sūcaiḥ sakale yathā nyāsāt śrutam tvayā śṛṇudhvam ṛṣayaḥ sarve sva icchā līlām maheśituḥ kṣobhyam viśvam idam tena kṣobhakaḥ bhagavant aśivaḥ saḥ saṃkoca vikāśābhyām pradhāna tve vyavasthitaḥ kṣobhyamānāt pradhānāt ca puṃsaḥ prādurabhūt vijāḥ yat etat vistṛtam bījam pradhāna puruṣa ātmakam buddhi ādayaḥ viśeṣa antāḥ avyaktāt īśvara icchyā puruṣa adhiṣṭhitāt eva jajñire muni puṃgavāḥ tatas jajñe tanmātrāṇi tatas dvijāḥ tatas bhūtāni jātāni preritāni śiva icchayā vaikārikāt ahaṃkārāt sargaḥ vaikārikaḥ bhavet taijasāni indriyāṇi āhuḥ devāḥ vaikārikāḥ daśa vaikārikāt taijesaḥ ca tāmasaḥ bhūtādeḥ abhavat sargaḥ bhūta tanmātra saṃjñitaḥ ha vikurvāṇaḥ tu bhūtondiḥ śabda mātram sasarja ha ākāśaḥ jāyate tasmāt tasya śabdaḥ guṇaḥ mataḥ pavanaḥ ca vikurvāṇaḥ rūpa mātram sasarja ha tejaḥ śva utpadyate tasmāt rūpam tasya guṇam viduḥ tejaḥ tu eva vikurvāṇam rasa mātram abhūt tatas utpadyante tatas ca apaḥ rasaḥ tāsām guṇaḥ mataḥ gandhāt ca pṛthivī jātā gandhaḥ tasyāḥ tu vai guṇaḥ śabda mātram yat ākāśam sparśa mātram samādṛṇot dviguṇaḥ procyate vāyuḥ śabda sparśa ātmakaḥ smṛtaḥ tathā eva viyantaḥ rūpam śabda sparśaḥ guṇau ubhau tejaḥ tatas syāt triguṇam sa śabda sparśa rūpavat rasa mātram guṇāḥ sarve trayaḥ ādyāḥ samāviśan apaḥ caturguṇāḥ tena gandha mātram samāviśan tasmāt pañca guṇā bhūmiḥ balā bhūteṣu kathyate puruṣa dhiṣṭhita tvāt ca avyakta anugrahena ca mahat ādi viśeṣa antāḥ hi aṇḍam utpādayanti te tasmin kāryam ca karaṇam saṃsiddham parameṣṭhinaḥ prākṛte aṇḍe viriñciḥ tu kṣetrajñaḥ brahma saṃjñitaḥ ādikartā sa bhūtānām brahmā agre samavartata meruḥ ulbam bhavet tasya jarāyuḥ ca api parvatāḥ āsan tatra abhavat viprāḥ sa deva asura mānuṣam adbhiḥ daśaguṇābhiḥ tu bāhyatas aṇḍam samāhṛtam apaḥ daśaguṇena eva tejasā bahis āvṛtāḥ tejaḥ daśaguṇena eva bāhyatas vāyunā āvṛtam māyuḥ kham tu bhūtādinā āvṛtam mahantā ca eva bhūtādiḥ avyaktena ās svṛtaḥ mahant etaiḥ āvaraṇaiḥ aṇḍam saptabhiḥ prākṛtaiḥ vṛtam guṇāḥ kāla vaśāt eva bhavanti viṣamāḥ samāḥ brahmāṇḍam eva vipra indrāḥ brahmanaḥ kṣetram ucyate kṣetrajñaḥ ca saḥ eva uktaḥ viriñciḥ ca prajāpatiḥ sahasra koṭayaḥ santi brahmāṇḍāḥ tiryañc ūrdhva jāḥ śūlinaḥ brahmāṇḍānām asaṃkhyānām brahma viṣṇu hara ātmanām na karaṇam kārya kriyā vā vidyate dvijāḥ sva icchayā bhagavant īśaḥ krīḍati avijayā saha kathitaḥ prākṛtaḥ sargaḥ saṃkṣepāt muni puṃgavāḥ abuddhi pūrvakaḥ tu eṣa brāhmā sṛṣṭiḥ atha ucyate iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde prākṛtasargakathanam nāma ekaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ saṃvibhāga ratāḥ krūrāḥ te parigrāhinaḥ smṛtāḥ ete pañca samākhyātāḥ sargāḥ devena bhānunā mahantaḥ prathamaḥ sargaḥ jñātavyaḥ brahmanaḥ dvijāḥ tanmātrāṇām dvitīyaḥ tu bhūta sargaḥ saḥ ucyate iti eṣa prākṛtaḥ sargaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ buddhi pūrvakaḥ caturthaḥ mukhya sargaḥ tu mukhyāḥ vai sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ tathā ūrdhvaśrotasām ṣaṣṭhaḥ deva sargaḥ tu saḥ smṛtaḥ tatas arvākśrotasām sargaḥ saptamaḥ sa tu mānuṣaḥ tamaḥ bhautikaḥ sargaḥ bhūta ādīnām dvijocamāḥ navamaḥ ca eva kaumāraḥ prākṛtāḥ vaikṛtāḥ tu ime taḥ uvāca tatas sasarja bhagavant devaḥ asau ātmanaḥ sutān śaṃbhum sanatkumāram ca pañca etān padmasaṃbhavaḥ na sṛṣṭau dadhire buddhim śiva eka dhyāna tatparāḥ sṛṣṭau teṣu anapekṣeṣu moha āviṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥ prāṇa ātmakaḥ samudbhūtaḥ lalāṭāt brahmanaḥ haraḥ kena api hetunā vimāḥ sūrya koṭi sama prabhaḥ rodayitvā abja janmānam tasmāt rudraḥ iti smṛtaḥ anyāni sapta nāmāni śṛṇudhvam muni puṃgavāḥ bhavaḥ śarvaḥ tathā īśānaḥ paśūnām patiḥ eva ca bhīma ugraḥ mahādevaḥ iti nāmāni sattamāḥ bhūmiḥ apaḥ analaḥ vāyu vyom sūrya candramāḥ tatra aṣṭamī dīkṣitaḥ tatra mūrtiḥ īśasya śūlinaḥ yābhiḥ vyāptam idam viśvam viśvasya asya jagat mayaḥ tena viśveśvaraḥ devaḥ iti nāmnā śivaḥ smṛtaḥ prajāḥ sṛja iti nirdiṣṭaḥ candramauliḥ viraścinā sasarja manasā rudrān ātma tulyān maheśvaraḥ nīla kaṇṭhān tri netrān ca jaṭā mukuṭa maṇḍitān vṛṣadhvajān vīta rāgān jarā maraṇa varjitān sarvajña śata koṭīn tān sarva anugrāhiṇaḥ parān dṛṣṭvā tān vividhān rudrān viraściḥ mām āha śaṃkaram mā sṛjaḥ prajām sṛjasva anyām sureśānaiḥ prajām mṛtyu samanvitām brahmānam abravīt śambhuḥ na asti mama tādṛśā prajā tatas prabhṛti viśvātmā na prāsūta śubhāḥ prajāḥ rudraiḥ ātma samudbhūtaiḥ krīḍā yuktaḥ tadā abhavat yasmāt sthitaḥ sthāṇuḥ iti smṛtaḥ jñānam vairāgyam aiśvarya tapaḥ satyam kṣamā dhṛtiḥ draṣṭṛ tvam ātma sambodhaḥ vaṣiṣṭhātṛ tvam eva ca śaṃkare saḥ eva bhagavant īśaḥ viśveśaḥ nīlalohitaḥ tatas tam āha bhagavān brahmā saṃvīkṣya śaṃkaram evam viśveśvaram śambhum samābhāṣya caturmukhaḥ stotreṇa anena tuṣṭāva śirasi ādhāya ca añjalim namaḥ śivāya devāya namaḥ te brahma rūpiṇe māheśvarī tubhyam tasmai vāyu ātmane namaḥ sṛjati aśeṣam eva idam yaḥ sva karma anurūpatas yaḥ śete śeṣa śayane viśvam āvṛtya māyayā namaḥ brahmāṇḍam yaḥ akhila ādhāram tasmai śeṣa ātmane namaḥ yaḥ parānte para ānandam pītvā divya eka sākṣiṇam yaḥ antarā sarva bhūtānām niyantā tiṣṭhati īśvaraḥ tam sarvasākṣiṇam devam namaḥ te paramātmane yasya keśeṣu jīmūtāḥ nadyaḥ sarva aṅga saṃdhiṣu yam vinidrāḥ yata śvāsāḥ saṃtuṣṭāḥ sama darśinaḥ bhuvaḥ paśyanti yuñjānāḥ tasyai yoga ātmane namaḥ yasya bhāsā vibhāti idam tat aham tamasaḥ param tattvam sadā nirākāram cit rūpam pārameśvaram yayā saṃtarate māyām yogī saṃkṣīṇa kalmaṣaḥ tasmai vidyā ātmane namaḥ yaḥ śete śeṣa śayane viśvam āvṛtya māyayā namaḥ brahmāṇḍam tasmai śeṣa ātmane namaḥ yaḥ parānte para ānandam pītvā divya eka sākṣiṇam yaḥ antarā sarva bhūtānām niyantā tiṣṭhati īśvaraḥ tam sarvasākṣiṇam devam namaḥ te paramātmane yasya keśeṣu jīmūtāḥ nadyaḥ sarva aṅga saṃdhiṣu yam vinidrāḥ yata śvāsāḥ saṃtuṣṭāḥ sama darśinaḥ bhāsate yuñjānāḥ tasmai yoga ātmane namaḥ yasya bhāsā vibhāti idam tat aham tamasaḥ param tattvam sadā nirākāram cit rūpam pārameśvaram yayā saṃtarate māyām yogī saṃkṣīṇa kalmaṣaḥ tasmai vidyā ātmane namaḥ nitya ānandam nirādhāram niṣkalam paramam śivam evam stutvā mahādevam brahmā tad bhāva bhāvitaḥ prāñjaliḥ praṇataḥ tasthau gṛṇan brahma sanātanam aiśvaryam brahma sadbhāvam vairāgyam ca dadau haraḥ parābhyām su śubhābhyām ca upaspṛśya maheśvaraḥ vyājahāra tvam idānīm mama ādeśāt sṛjasva vividhāḥ prajāḥ sarga rakṣā laya guṇaiḥ nirguṇaḥ aham na saṃśayaḥ sa tvam mama agratas putraḥ sṛṣṭi hetoḥ vinirmitaḥ dakṣiṇāt aṅgāt vāma aṅgāt puruṣottamaḥ hṛdayāt udraḥ saṃjātaḥ kāma rūpa dhṛka brahma viṣṇu hara ākhyānām yaḥ paraḥ parameśvaraḥ tam mahāntam mahādevam brahman jānanti sūrayaḥ evam brahmānam ābhāṣya dattvā ca vividhān varān tatas ca pāśa vicchittiḥ śivaḥ eva bhavet tatas iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde harotpattyādikathanam nāma trayoviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ na ūcuḥ katham sa bhagavant sarvasya ādyaḥ api san vibhuḥ taḥ uvāca āsīt ekārṇave ghore naṣṭe vai sacarācare nārāyaṇaḥ mahā yogī śete tasmin tamas maye yoganidrām samāsādya śeṣa ahi śayane dvijāḥ brahmā jagāma tam deśam puruṣottamaḥ samutthāpya ca tam brahmā madhusūdanam māyayā moḍitām brahmā sureśvaram brūhi iti ukte abravīt viṣṇuḥ brahmānam tejasām nidhiḥ na jānāsi katham mūḍha mām antaryāmiṇam vibhum sarvasya āyam suraśreṣṭham jānīhi iti abravīt vibhuḥ kaḥ bhavān iti tam prāha brahmā harim atha abravīt aham vai sarva bhūtānām ādyaḥ sarva jagat patiḥ brahmānam mām param devam jānīhi puruṣa ṛṣabhaiḥ carācara ātmakam viśvam mayi tiṣṭhati sarvadā praviṣṭaḥ brahmanaḥ deham tatra lokān dadarśa saḥ sahasra śīrṣā puruṣaḥ punar brahmāṇam abravīt carācara ātmakāḥ lokān sa deva asura mānuṣān praviśya bhuvanān sarvān dṛṣṭvā abhūt vismitaḥ vidhiḥ na apaśyat nirgamaiḥ dvāram pihitāni ca catriṇā tam abravīt gadā pāṇiḥ brahmānam amita dyutiḥ līlā artham etat sakalam pitāmahaiḥ kṛtam mayā na mātsaryāt suraśreṣṭha dvāra rodhaḥ mayā kṛtaḥ tvam eva jagantaḥ mānyaḥ sarvasya ādyaḥ pitāmahaḥ tatas svayambhuḥ viśva ādi śvakriṇe varam uttamam tatas tam abravīt viṣṇum na āvābhyām vidyate param tvad mayam mad mayam sarvam ekā mūrtiḥ dvidhā sthitā evam nigaditaḥ viṣṇuḥ brahmanā parameṣṭhinā kim na paśyasi viśveśam svayam jyotiḥ sanātanam param devam adhikam śaraṇam vidhe evam hareḥ nigaditam śrutvā brahmā tam abravīt nau adhikaḥ kaścid vidyeta iti mudhā hare bhāṣase nidrayā assu iṣṭaḥ tyaja moham mahāmate uvāca mā evam vidhe yat a jñātvā param bhāvam maheśvare asti iti na anyathā aham te bravīmi kamalāsanaiḥ mohita ātmā na saṃdehaḥ māyayā parameṣṭhinaḥ māyī viśva ātmakaḥ rudraḥ māyā śaktiḥ tu śāṃkarā ka kha ma vaḍa ca saṃjñita pustakeṣu viṣṇuḥ uvāca iti na asti sadā janānām hṛdaye saṃniviṣṭaḥ api yaḥ paraiḥ yaḥ tu kāla ātma yuktāni kāraṇāni api līlayā tad ananta śaktiḥ aikātmā bhagavant adhitiṣṭhati yasya śambhoḥ parā śaktiḥ bhāva gamyā manoharā nirguṇā sva guṇaiḥ eva nigūḍhā niṣkalā śivā ayam ādiḥ anādi antaḥ svabhāvāt eva nirmalaḥ tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tat tatra anantaḥ paripūrṇaḥ ca sva icchā adhīnaḥ śvara acaraḥ tadīyam trividham rūpam sthūla sūkṣmam tatas param asmat ādyaiḥ suraiḥ dṛśyam sthūlam sūkṣmam tu yogibhiḥ prasādāt eva sā bhaktiḥ prasādaḥ bhakti sambhavaḥ yathā iha aṅkurāt bījam bījāt vā yathā aṅkuraḥ tasya prasāda leśena paśoḥ pāśa parikṣayaḥ tasmāt paśupatiḥ śambhuḥ paśavaḥ tu asmat ādayaḥ sarveṣām mukti daḥ śambhuḥ teṣām bhāva anurūpatas paraḥ bhūtvā punar āvartya mucyate tasmāt na eka prakāreṇa narāṇām muktiḥ iṣyate jñāna bhāva anurūpeṇa prasādena eva nirvṛtiḥ tvam ekā bhagavat mūrtiḥ anyā nārāyaṇī parā raudrī tṛtīyā kathitā jagat saṃhāra kāriṇī etāsām prerakaḥ śambhuḥ svam sve kārye caturmukhaiḥ nirguṇaḥ api guṇa adhyakṣaḥ svatantra aiśvarya vigrahaḥ tam īśvaram mahādevam na paśyasi katham vidhe divyam dadāmi te cakṣuḥ yena paśyasi tam śivam brahmā labdhvā param jñānam aiśvaram nirguṇam param tam eva śaraṇam gatvā saṃstūya vividhaiḥ stavaiḥ prītaḥ bhūtvā mahādevaḥ caturmukham atha abravīt tvām eva putram icchāmi tvayā vā sadṛśam sutam tvad māyā mohitaḥ śambho na vedmi tvā param śivam namāmi te pāda abjam yoginām bhava bheṣajam śrutvā viraścaiḥ vacanam devadevaḥ pinākadhṛk brahmānam abravīt putram samālokya atha cakriṇam mad viṣayam kṣipram bhaviṣyati te anagha eṣa yogi īśvaraḥ śāṅga mama eva aṃśaḥ na saṃśayaḥ sāhāyye bhavitā brahman mama ādeśāt te anaghaiḥ evam dattvā varam śambhu brahmane dvijasattamāḥ atha abravīt hṛṣīkeśam prāñjalim puratas sthitam varam varaya dāsyāmi te nārāyaṇa avyaya mad jñāna jñeya ātmakam viśvam tvad mayam mad mayam hare hi jñātā aham jñāna rūpaḥ tvam mantā aham tvam matire prakṛtiḥ tvam suraśreṣṭhaiḥ puruṣaḥ aham na saṃśayaḥ tvam candramāḥ aham sūryaḥ śarvarī tvam aham dinam tvam eva māyā viśvasya māyā aham paramaiḥ vibho brahmā uvāca ini 6ṅaca ṅasajñi pustakeṣu na asti evam śambhoḥ vacaḥ śrutvā vāsudevaḥ nirañjanaḥ abravīt paramātmānam mahādevam dvijottamāḥ uvāca evam astu iti atha ābhāṣya ca śārṅgiṇam pālaya etat mama ādeśāt iti uktvā antarhitaḥ haraḥ tathā sarvam aśeṣeṇa kathitam muni puṃgavāḥ katham bhagavatī gaurī śaṃkara ardha śarīriṇī ūcuḥ para brahma ātmakā nityā paramā ākāśa madhya gā sarva śakti mayā śāntā nirguṇā nirupadravā svar bhābhiḥ bhāsayantīm viśvam etat sureśvarī nitya ānandā nirātaṅkā nirvibhāgā nirañjanā pṛthak śarīram akarot katham sā parameśvarī taḥ uvāca labdhvā prajāḥ sasarja bhagavān na vyavardhanta tāḥ prajāḥ duḥkhitaḥ abhūt tadā brahmā prajāḥ dṛṣṭvā tu durbalāḥ mene akṛtārtham ātmānam prādurbhūtaḥ tatas haraḥ brahmānam abravīt śambhuḥ jñātam tvad duḥkha kāraṇam hanārīśvaraḥ devaḥ svayam viśveśvaraḥ śivaḥ nārī bhāgān mahādevaḥ sasarja pṛthak īśvarām brahma ātmakām parām śakti koṭi vāla arka bhāsurām bhū bhū bhū bhū bhū bhū bhū bhū bhū bhū bhū bhū bhū bhū bhū bhū brahma indra viṣṇu namitā ṣṭa mūrti aṅginīm ajām pradhāna puruṣa atītām sāvitrīm vedamātaram bhṛgu yajuḥ sāma nilayām ṛjum kuṇḍalinīm parām viśveśvarīm viśva mayīm viśveśvara prativratām sarga sthiti anta kāriṇī vyakta avyakta svarūpiṇīm pāhi mām devadeveśaiḥ śaraṇa āgata vatsale tvam mātā mama kalyāṇe pitā sarva īśvaraḥ śivaḥ mṛṣṭaḥ aham tripura ghnena sṛṣṭi arthaiḥ śaṃkara priye prajāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ na vṛddhim upayānti tāḥ tatas param prajāḥ sarvāḥ maithuna prabhavāḥ kila saṃvadhātum icchāmi kṛtvā sṛṣṭim atas param kṛtvā sṛṣṭim atas param śaktīn om khalu sarvāsām tvattaḥ sṛṣṭiḥ mṛttate tat kulam śive sarveṣām dehinām devi sarva śakti pradāyinī sṛṣṭi vivṛddhi artham aṃśena ekena śāśvate mām arthitā vai tadā devī brahmanā muni puṃgavāḥ ekām śaktim bhruvoḥ madhyāt sasarja ātma sama prabhām mahasan prekṣya devīm viśveśvaraḥ haraḥ mādāya śirasā śambhoḥ ājñā sā parameśvarī abhavat dakṣa duhitrī kha icchayā brahma rūpiṇī punar ādyā parā śaktiḥ śambho deham samāviśat ardhanārīśvaraḥ devaḥ vibhāti iti hi naḥ śrutiḥ tatas prabhṛti vipra indrāḥ maithuna prabhavāḥ prajāḥ evam vaḥ kathitāḥ devyāḥ sambhūtiḥ uttamā paṭhet yaḥ śṛṇuyāt vā api saṃtatiḥ tasya vardhate iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde gaurīpṛthaśarīratvādikathanam nāma pañcaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ taḥ uvāca asṛjat bhagavān brahmā marīci ādīn kalmaṣān dakṣam atrim vasiṣṭham ca saḥ asajat manasā vibhuḥ deva asura manuṣyān ca pitṛ śāpi prajāpatiḥ asṛjat kramaśas sarvān andhakāre ca rākṣasān gandhaiḥ sa tathā nāgān yakṣān ca api sahasraśas asṛjan pukhatas vimān dāhubhyām kṣatriyān viḥ ūru dvayāt tathā vaiśyān pādāt śūdrān sasarja ha chandāṃsi vedān yajñān atha kalpasūtram atas param vedāṅgāni tatas sṛṣṭvā maithuna prabhavām śraddhā ādīnām dvijottamāḥ kardamam ca ambarīṣam ca pulahāt suṣuve kṣamā durvāsasam tathā somam dattātreyam ca yoginam sinīvālī kuhūm ca eva rākām anumatim tathā putrīḥ sūte lakṣaṇa saṃyutāḥ mītau pulastyāt abhavat dattaḥ nirmānavaiḥ sutaḥ pūrva janmāni yaḥ agastyaḥ khyātaḥ svāyambhuve antare putrāṇām ṣaṣṭi sāhasram saṃtatiḥ suṣuve kratoḥ saṃtatau teṣām catvāriṃśat pañca ca pāvaka ādyāḥ traya vā ete catvāriṃśat tathā nava yajñeṣu bhāginaḥ sarve tathā sarve tapasvinaḥ rudra arcana pare sarve tripuṇḍra aṅkita mastakāḥ ayajvānaḥ ca yajvānaḥ pitaraḥ brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ agniṣvāttāḥ barhiṣadaḥ dvidhā teṣām vyavasthitiḥ menām ca dhāriṇīm tatra yoga mārga rate ubhe menā himavantaḥ sūte mainākam krauñcam eva ca mentum dhāriṇī sūte mandaram cāru kandaram dhāriṇī suṣuve velām niyantim ca āyatim tathā sāgarāt suṣuve velā sāmudrīm nāma nāmnaḥ prācīnavarhiṣā sā ca daśa putrān ajījanat prācetasaḥ iti khyātāḥ sarve svāyambhuve antare matra śāpāt abhūt putraḥ yeṣām dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ atha idānīm manoḥ putra saṃtatim kathayāmi vaḥ taḥ uvāca uttānapādasya sutaḥ dhruvaḥ nāma mahā manāḥ mad bhagavant parama devam nārāyaṇam anāmayam nirmamaḥ nirahaṃkāraḥ tān niṣṭhaḥ tad parāyaṇaḥ dhruvasya putrāḥ catvāraḥ sṛṣṭiḥ dhanyat tathā paraḥ haryaḥ śambhuḥ mahātmānaḥ vaiṣṇavāḥ prathita ojasaḥ chāyā pañca sutān sūte sṛṣṭeḥ dharma parāyaṇaun ripum ripuṃjayam vipram ṣalam katejasam ripoḥ bhāryā tu bṛhatī prasūte cakṣuṣam sutam sūte puṣkariṇī putram cakṣuṣā ākṣuṣam manum tad vaṃśa jāḥ asaṃkhyātāḥ tuśiva ādayaḥ khyātaḥ sa pṛthivīpālaḥ yena dugdhā vasuṃdharā mītaḥ tam abravīt viṣṇuḥ pṛthum muni vara uttamāḥ āsthāya paramām bhakti bhagavant ait vācam āśritaḥ pṛthoḥ bhāryā mahābhāgā kālena suṣuve sutau jikhaṇḍinam havirdhānam suśīlaḥ ca śikhaṇḍinaḥ hi aśvatara nāmānam śiva dhyāna eka tatparam upāsya labdhavan taramā suśīlaḥ yogam aiśvaram bhagavantaḥ ūcuḥ suśīlena katham rājñā prāptam jñānam anuttamam taḥ uvāca yaḥ asau śikhaṇḍinaḥ putraḥ brahmacarya āśrame rataḥ apaśyat yogibhiḥ juṣṭam mahādeva kṛta ālayam yatra siddhāḥ mahātmānaḥ marīci ādyāḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ ca bhagavant tathā ca anye sura asurāḥ samārādhya mahādevam siddhim prāptāḥ hi anekaśas yatra mandākinī gaṅgā rājate hi agha hāriṇī apaśyat āśramam tasyāḥ tīre yogi indra sevitam dhyāyamānaḥ kṣaṇam tatra sthitaḥ viśveśvaram śivam mahā aśvatara nāmānam atha apaśyat mahā munim mahāpāśupatam śāntam jīrṇa kaupīna vāsasam bhasma uddhūlita sarva aṅgam tripuṇḍra tilaka anvitam abhivandya muneḥ pādau śirasā prāñjaliḥ nṛpaḥ abravīt tam muni śreṣṭham sarva bhūta anukampinam tapāṃsi saphalāni eva jātāni tava darśanāt bhavāmi tatra śiṣyaḥ aham rakṣa saṃsāra jāt bhayāt rājānam muni puṃgavāḥ bhaya niṣṭhaḥ jita indriyaḥ saṃnyāsa vidhim āśritya suśīlaḥ muktimān bhavet iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde uttānapāda saṃtatyādi kathanam nāma saviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ taḥ uvāca tu ayaṃbhuvā samāviṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥ prajāḥ sṛja iti rugadī ca sura asurān ṣaṣṭim dakṣaḥ asṛjat kanyāḥ asikayām vai prajāpatiḥ saptaviṃśatim somāya catatraḥ ariṣṭanemine dve ca eva bahuputrāya dve kṛśāśvāya dhīmate dve ca eva aṅgirase tat vadau dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ sādhyā viśvā ca saṃkalpā muhūrtī ca hi arundhatī marutvatī vasuḥ bhānuḥ lambā jāmī iti tāḥ daśa sādhyāḥ babhūvuḥ sādhyāyām viśvāyām viśva devatāḥ saṃkalpāyāntu saṃkalpaḥ muhūrta jāḥ atu lamdāyām ghoṣa nāmānaḥ nāgavīthīḥ tu jāmī jāḥ samākhyātāḥ sarva bhūta hita eṣiṇaḥ malaḥ ca somavant anilaḥ analaḥ matyūpaḥ ca prabhāsaḥ ca vasavaḥ aṣṭa prakīrtitāḥ upāsya labdhavan taramā suśīlaḥ yogam aiśvaram ṛyaḥ ūcuḥ suśīlena katham rājñā prāptam jñānam anuttamam taḥ uvāca yaḥ asau śikhaṇḍinaḥ brahmacarya āśrame rataḥ apaśyat yogibhiḥ juṣṭam mahādeva kṛta ālayam yatra siddhāḥ mahātmānaḥ marīci ādyāḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ ca bhagavant tathā ca anye sura asurāḥ samārādhya mahādevam siddhim prāptāḥ hi anekaśas yatra mandākinī gaṅgā rājate hi agha hāriṇī apaśyat āśramam tasyāḥ tīre yogi indra sevitam dhyāyamānaḥ kṣaṇam tatra sthitaḥ viśveśvaram śivam mahā aśvatara nāmānam atha apaśyat mahā munim mahāpāśupatam śāntam jīrṇa kaupīna vāsasam bhasma uddhūlita sarva aṅge tripuṇḍu tilaka anvitam abhivandya muneḥ pādau śirasā prāñjaliḥ nṛpaḥ abravīt tam muni śreṣṭham sarva bhūta anukampinam tapāṃsi saphalāni eva jātāni tava darśanāt bhavāmi tava śiṣyaḥ aham rakṣa saṃsāra jāt bhayāt rājānam muni gavāḥ bhaya niṣṭhaḥ jita indriyaḥ iti śrī brahmaṇā uṣa rāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde uttānapāda saṃtatyādi kathanam nāma saha viṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ taḥ uvāca svayambhunā samāviṣṭaḥ pūrva dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ prajāḥ sṛja iti rūk īdau rururja ca sura asurān prajāpateḥ aṇasya kanyā ari nīti ditā ṣaṣṭim dakṣaḥ asṛjat kanyāḥ vai prajāpatiḥ saptaviṃśatim somāya catas ariṣṭanemine dve ca eva bahuputrāya dve kṛśāśvāya dhīmate ca eva aṅgirase tat vadau dakṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ sādhyā viśvā ca saṃkalpā muhūrtā ca hi arundhatī marutvatī vasuḥ bhānuḥ lambā jāmī iti tāḥ daśa sādhyāḥ babhūvuḥ sādhyāyām viśvāyām viśva devatāḥ saṃkalpāyāḥ tu saṃkalpaḥ gṛhatīta murta jāḥ masoḥ tu vasavaḥ proktāḥ bhānoḥ te bhānavaḥ smṛtāḥ lambāyām ghoṣa nāmānaḥ nāgavīthīḥ tu jāmī jāḥ samākhyātāḥ xc-9 se-9 mahā apaḥ nalaḥ ca somaḥ ca dhruvaḥ ca eva anilaḥ analaḥ pratyūṣaḥ ca prabhāsaḥ ca vasavaḥ aṣṭa prakīrtitāḥ tu ariṣṭā surasā proktā svadhā surabhiḥ eva ca vinatā ca tathā tāmrā kodhavaśā virā aṃśuḥ dhātā bhagaḥ tvaṣṭā mitraḥ atha varuṇaḥ aryamā ca tuṣitāḥ nāma te cānuṣasya antare manoḥ mādityāḥ adityāḥ putrāḥ proktāḥ vaivasvate antare putra dvayam ditiḥ sūte kaśyapāt muni puṃgavāt hiraṇyakaśipum tu ekam hiraṇyākṣam anantaram śaka ādyāḥ devatāḥ sarvāḥ tena daityena vādhitāḥ brahmānam śaraṇam gatvā procuḥ prāñjalayaḥ surāḥ hiraṇyakena daityena śastrān traiḥ sūditāḥ vayam dārāḥ ca apahṛtāḥ tena vajra ādīni āyudhāni ca trāyasva asmān rbhaya trastān śaraṇam na anyat asti naḥ evam suraiḥ nigaditam śrutvā ca eva pitāmahaḥ devaiḥ saha yayau tūrṇam viṣṇuḥ avyayaḥ bādhate sakalān devān munīn nirdhūta kalmaṣān yaḥ tam haniṣyati kṣipram na tam paśyāmi mādhavaiḥ hantum arhasi tam śīghram devānām kārya siddhaye śrutvā nārāyaṇaḥ vākyam īritam tridivaukasām narasya ardha tanum kṛtvā siṃhasya ardha tanum tathā nṛsiṃha rūpī bhagavant hiraṇyakaśipoḥ pure bhagavant devaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ muñcan nādam mahā ghoram asurāṇām bhayaṃkaram hiraṇyakaśipuḥ dṛṣṭvā nṛsiṃham ati bhīpaṇam saṃhādaḥ hādaḥ eva ca hiraṇyakaśipoḥ putrāḥ catvāraḥ prathita ojasaḥ te sārdham yuyudhuḥ dānavāḥ tadā prahlādaḥ prāhiṇot rāhmam astram tam narakesarim tathā prāhiṇot vāde āgneyam tathā ca anye mahā asurāḥ catvāri iyāṇi saṃprāpya bhagavantam nṛkesarim babhūvuḥ tāni bhagnāni yathā vajra āhatāḥ dumaḥ gṛhītvā caturaḥ putrān hastābhyām narakesariḥ cikṣepa gaganāt bhūmau gṛhītvā evam punar punar evam tān vyathitān dṛṣṭvā hiraṇyakaśipuḥ svayam vinivṛttaḥ aśvaiḥ saṃgrāmāt prahādaḥ daitya rāj tatas jñātvā tu bhagavat bhāvam nṛsiṃha tyā amita ojasaḥ dhyātvā ām nārāyaṇam devam vārayāmāsa dānavān eṣa nārāyaṇaḥ yogī parama ātmā sanātanaḥ putra uditam an ādṛtya hiraṇyakaśipuḥ punar yuyudhe hariṇā sārdham yāvat varṣa śataṃtryam atha viśvātmakaḥ viṣṇuḥ krodha saṃrakta locanaḥ nakhaiḥ vidārayāmāsa hiraṇyakaśipum tadā iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde surāsurasṛṣṭyādikathanam nāma aṣṭāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca hiraṇyākṣam mahā bāhum rājye samabhiyojayat devān raṇe jitvā vai palāyitāḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ mahādevam tapasā ārādhya ca antakam lebhe putram mahā bāhum sarva amara niṣūdanam hiraṇyākṣa bhayāt devāḥ śārṅgiṇam śaraṇam gatāḥ dṛṣṭvā atha bhagavant devān hiraṇyākṣa vadhāya vai vārāham rūpam āsthāya hiraṇyākṣaḥ niṣūditaḥ te tasmin hiraṇyākṣe prahlādaḥ vaiṣṇava agraṇī tyaktvā tu tāmasā vṛttim svakīyam rājyam āsthitaḥ tatas kadācid devānām māyayā mohitaḥ abhavat paścana brāhmaṇam dṛṣṭvā kṛśa aṅgam gṛham āgatam avajñām akarot daityaḥ śaptaḥ tena agrajanmanā iti śaptvā yayau vipraḥ sva āśramam muni puṃgavāḥ pituḥ vadham anusmṛtya deva aśvāḥ ye vinirjitāḥ anugrahāt bhagavantaḥ pūrvāt aitya rāj punar tyaktvā māyā mayam sarve śārṅgiṇam śaraṇam yayau atha devaḥ mahādevaḥ śaraṇyaḥ sarva dehinām kena api hetunā bhikṣām akarot rāhmaṇaiḥ saha saṃsthāpya mandare devīm girijām girijāpatiḥ sa nārāyaṇakān devān akarot pārśvaga āśivaḥ strī prītaḥ asmi te dāsyāmi gāṇapatyam hi durlabham nandīśvara samaḥ vatsa bhṛṅgī nāma gaṇaḥ bhava nīlakaṇṭha sinetraḥ ca vṛṣaketuḥ jaṭādharaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā devatāḥ sarvāḥ harṣa nirbhara mānasāḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ gaṇa
