prahasan kamala īkṣaṇām maheśvaraḥ uvāca hanu devaiḥ mahābhāge yat vṛttam tat ravīmi aham śive yathā mama varavarṇini devāḥ mad śaraṇam prāptāḥ na ca aham śaraṇam tyaje gopyāḥ mayā sadā kānte mahādevaḥ rataḥ smṛtaḥ bhaviṣyati mahābhāge putraḥ te ṣaḍānanaḥ tu aurasaḥ tu suśroṇi devaiḥ teṣṭaḥ tava aṃśāt tasmāt śuddham mayā retaḥ mukhe vai jātavedasaḥ vahni kukṣi gatam retaḥ gatam devān vibhāgaśaḥ tāḥ kṛttikāḥ ṣaḍ samākhyātāḥ gaṅgāyām snātum āgatāḥ tatas tāḥ kṛttikāḥ stabdhāḥ devi mām śaraṇam gatāḥ mahādevam sthitā devī iti naḥ śrutam iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde pāvakastutyādikathanam nāma ekaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sagarbhāḥ khalu saṃjātāḥ devadevena śambhunā kim akurveḥ tadā sarve nārāyaṇa purogamāḥ etat sarve samāsena brūhi naḥ sūtaiḥ pṛcchatām taḥ uvāca daśa pañca sahasrāṇām atīteṣu dvijottamāḥ ca tathā ca duḥkhitāḥ pārvatī kāntam śaṃkaram śaraṇam yayuḥ ūcuḥ prāñjalayaḥ sarve sūrya koṭi sama prabham bhagavan yat idam duḥkham garbha jam deha śoṣaṇam śaṃkara upahāsyam idam deva puṃsām yat garbha sambhavaḥ mad bhava devānām kara ālambam dadasva naḥ tāre praṇata ārti vināśanaiḥ evam śru tu vacana deva pārvatīpati īṣat vihasya bhagavant uvāca idam sureśvaraḥ maheśvaraḥ uvāca bhavat hiḥ īdṛśam kāryam iṣṭam vai sura puṃgavāḥ na iṣṭam devyaḥ dara ratham hi tasmāt garbha daśām gatāḥ idānīm yat prakartavyam śṛṇudhvam tat sura uttamāḥ mad dhāna vane yūyam idā utsaṅge prasūyata tatas śambhoḥ vacaḥ śrutvā nārāyaṇa purogamāḥ nārāyaṇam puraskṛtya prasūtāḥ sarva devatāḥ asti śārveṇa tejasā tena rañjitaḥ meru parvataḥ tatas kāñcana tām prāptaḥ sa śaila vana kānanaḥ tasmāt jarā ādibhiḥ muktāḥ amarāḥ ca sura uttamāḥ sarve kāñcana saṃkāśāḥ saṃjātāḥ tad prabhāvataḥ gaṅgāyām nihitam yat ca tat ekastham abhūt vijāḥ tat tejaḥ piṅgalam prekṣya śaṃkaraḥ varṣāṇām ca sahastreṇa kaṭhinam skanda tām gataḥ skandaḥ kumāraḥ ṣaḍvaktraḥ tathā dvādaśalocanaḥ haiḥ dvādaśabhiḥ ca eva śobhamānaḥ abhavat tadā ha īśa ādeśāt punar strātum kṛttikāḥ parama ujjvalāḥ tābhiḥ kṣīram yatas dattam kārttikeyaḥ iti smṛtaḥ garbha paṅka vilipta aṅga gaṅgāyām strāpitaḥ prabhuḥ tapta cāmīkara ābhāsaḥ śaradhāna vane tadā nāmnām sahasreṇa tadā kumāraḥ vedhasā stutaḥ bhedayitvā tu tat śṛṅgam śatadhā kṛtam siṃha ādayaḥ api tatrasthāḥ tena nādena sūditāḥ tatas tam krīḍamānam tu dṛṣṭvā devam śivātmajam piṅgalaḥ devadeveśam jñāpayāmāsa śaṃkaram paśya tvam devadeveśaiḥ krīḍamānam kumārakam sūrya ayuta pratīkāśam ātma sūnum ṣaḍānanam mamarda śambhoḥ ca bhujaṃga hāram jagrāha candram sa kaparda saṃstham pañcamyām sthāpitaḥ saḥ atha ṣaṣṭhayām ṣaṣṭhī priyaḥ guhaḥ catuṣpādavatīm tyaktvā trailokyam hantum udyataḥ abodhayat tadā bālaḥ jantūn sthāvara jaṅgamān kvacid śraṅgaḥ gireḥ śauryāt nayati āśu samāna tām kacid siṃhān samākṛṣya pātayāmāsa bhū tale āruhya abhyahanat pṛṣṭhe tān eva bhrāmayan punar kacid nāgau gṛhītvā tu karābhyām sammukhau ubhau tadā anyonyam kumbhābhyām saḥ ca līlayā samutpatya samādāya khecarāṇām umāsutaḥ tathā cikṣepa sahasā bālaḥ vimānāni avanī tale punar utpatya vegena prekṣyamāṇaḥ kha maṇḍale mārgaiḥ rurodha sūrya indroḥ grahānām ca tathā eva saḥ utpādaya meru śṛṅgāṇi saḥ akṣipat parvatān ca viśeṣeṇa nadīca unmārgāt anayat tatas te bhṛśam udvignāḥ śakram śatru pratāpanam ūcuḥ gatvā dvijaśreṣṭhāḥ bhūtāḥ vākyam idam tadā tava eṣa rājya hartā vai bhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ tathā utsāhāt ca tejasaḥ nūnam śataguṇena ayam adhikaḥ śreha dṛśyate kariṣyasi vacaḥ naḥ tava rājyam bhaviṣyati upekṣā na eva kartavyā śiśum matvā puraṃdaraiḥ uvāca vacanam ślakṣṇam teṣām dharma parāyaṇam dharma ghnam pāpa saṃghātam kīrti ghnam vai carācare śrūyatām abhidhāsyāmi dharma śāstrasya niścitam mahā cara cara carācarāḥ māturam bhīrum udvignam ekastham śaraṇa āgatam patitam prapalāyantam kāma āsaktam nirāyudham sūdayiṣyanti ye nūnam mūḍhāḥ te naraka arṇavāt tasmāt vrajadhvam śaraṇam yatra śambhu sutaḥ guhaḥ evam ukte tu śakreṇa bhṛśa duḥkhitāḥ tad krodha saṃdīpanam vākyam punar ūcuḥ cara acarāḥ mad ayam ślokaḥ na asti bhūtāḥ ūcuḥ tadā nītiḥ gatā kutra dāruṇe garbha pātane kaḥ ca nāma naraḥ śūraḥ yaḥ bālam yodhayet raṇe purā mayā yathā garbhaḥ cara acarāḥ tathā idānīm nihanyate evam uktvā tatas śakraḥ krodha anala samīritaḥ ha ājñāpayat tadā viprāḥ sādhyān devān divākarān śaradhānam gamiṣyāmi vadha arthī bālakasya ca tad ādeśāt suraiḥ tūrṇam sarva āyudha samanvitaḥ niveditaḥ sa śakrāya tam āruhya puraṃdaraḥ sādhyaiḥ ca vasubhiḥ ca marut gaṇaiḥ mad yayau skanda vadhāya saḥ viyat maṇḍalam āsthāya stūyamānaḥ carācaraiḥ nṛtyamāna apsarobhiḥ ca vādyamānaiḥ ca kiṃnaraiḥ ca divyaiḥ jegīyamānaḥ sura kiṃnarībhiḥ pepīyamānaḥ sura sundarībhiḥ kāma āturābhiḥ nayanaiḥ ajasram saṃpūjyamānaḥ muni siddha saṃdhaiḥ mudā anvitaḥ vajra dharaḥ kirīṭī iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde parameśvarasurasaṃvādādikathanam nāma dviṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ taḥ uvāca evam gatvā sahasrākṣaḥ pārvatī sutaḥ bolam sūrya ayuta prakhyam tam apaśyat śacīpatiḥ malaya agni caya ākāram dṛṣṭvā nāradam abravīt idam kim bhāti devarṣe meroḥ śataguṇa ucchrayam evam śakra vacaḥ śrutvā bhagavān padmabhūsutaḥ airāvata gaja ārūḍham śacīpatim atha abravīt nāradaḥ uvāca tasya eva eṣa prabhāvaḥ ayam nūnam deva śatakrato bhāskarāṇām na pujaḥ ayam na eva parvata saṃcayaḥ bālena utpādyamānena saha devaiśva rañjitaḥ adhas yojana saṃkhyābhiḥ sahasrāṇi eva ṣoḍaśa caturaśītiḥ utsedhaḥ dvātriṃśat vistaraḥ smṛtaḥ gataḥ tat tejaḥ skandatām yātam sahasra abdaiḥ gataiḥ tathā caturthyā sa ākṛtiḥ devaiḥ pañcamyām aṅgavant tatas ṣaṣṭhayām padbhyām yathā trailokyam vijayiṣyati tvayā saha ayam saptamyām pālayiṣyati vā punar nānā praharaṇa upetam nānā ābharaṇa bhūṣitam mātṛbhiḥ gaṇa vṛndaiḥ ca sevyamānam umāsutam mumoca vṛtrāriḥ sphuliṅga udvāri bhīṣaṇam tṛṇa vat manyamānaḥ asau vajram tat pārvatīsutaḥ śareṇa ekena vivyādha papāne ca saḥ mūrchitaḥ punar anyam samādāya śaram jvalana saṃnibham chattram dhvajam patākāḥ ca hareḥ ciccheda ṣaṇmukhaḥ bheda anyena tīkṣṇena hastam vai vajriṇaḥ guhaḥ hareṇa āditya tulyena rurum śambhuḥ yathā āhave punar vāṇam samādāya tam jaghāna śatakratum apareṇa tu tīkṣṇena mukuṭam tu tathā hareḥ ca ca vibheda viṃśatyā vāyudevam ca ravim ca daśa pañcabhiḥ triṃśadbhiḥ somarājānam tāḍayitvā raṇe punar śakram pañcaśataiḥ āśu śaraiḥ śra prāṇa hāribhiḥ śūraḥ nādam pramuñcan vai śakram dudrāva śambhujaḥ hataḥ śaikhaka raivalaḥ siṃhaiḥ śarabha rāj iva tatas tān āgatān dṛṣṭvā deva śaṃkara vallabhaḥ kesarī iva mṛgān kṣudrān dudrāva ca divaukasaḥ punar skandam sahasrākṣaḥ vajreṇa tam atāḍayat tāḍite tu tatas tasmāt utpannāḥ cāru mūrtayaḥ devāḥ ca vedāḥ ca lokāḥ ca agni divākarāḥ deva mantrī mahā prājñaḥ vṛhaspatiḥ atha abravīt tava upadekṣye aham sahasrākṣaiḥ śṛṇuṣva tat anena saha samprītim kṛtvā rājyam akaṇṭakam bhuṅkṣva tvam niścalam kṛtvā dānavān ca niṣūdaya intavyaḥ sa katham śakraiḥ śata saṃkhyaiḥ bhavādṛśaiḥ taḥ uvāca śrutvā tasya vacaḥ śakraḥ tadā suraguroḥ dvijāḥ tam eva śaraṇam prāyāt kumāram pārvatī sutam prasīda me tvam śaraṇa āgatasya pādau navā śirasā vahāmi sura adhipaḥ tvam bhava śarva sūno gṛhāṇa rājyam mama śambhu kalpa ugram satām hi kopaḥ praṇateṣu nityam vināśam eti ārya manaḥ su siddham tat bravīt karuṇā āviṣṭaḥ śakram prati muni īśvarāḥ aparyāptam na mama kiṃcid asti pitroḥ prasādāt niṣkaṇṭakam tvam eva iha rājyam kuru śacīpate evam skanda vacaḥ śrutvā punar āha śacīpatiḥ bhagavan na aparaḥ kaścid evānām viditaḥ valī vālaḥ ka ca saṃgrāmaḥ ka nītiḥ ka parākramaḥ māyā ka ca dākṣiṇyam kka śāntiḥ ka prasāda tā sva rūpaiḥ sva guṇaiḥ tvam hi bandibhiḥ vāraṇaiḥ tathā yakṣaiḥ ca vividhaiḥ guṇa koṭibhiḥ stūyamānaḥ amaraiḥ siddhaiḥ gandharva apsarasām gaṇaiḥ tiṣṭhasva upari kṛtsnasya trailokyam bhuṅkṣva ṣaṇmukhaiḥ evam śakra vacaḥ śrutvā punar prāha ambikāsutaḥ abhayam śakraiḥ mā bhaiṣīḥ kuru rājyam akaṇṭakam handa udīrṇāḥ dānavāḥ ye ca tān tadā yaiḥ parājīyase atyarthe sūdaye aham tvayā smṛtaḥ punar atha uvāca mahādeva putram saṃvīkṣya niḥspṛham evam astu iti tam prāha kārttikeyaḥ śacīpatim tatas sarvaiḥ suraiḥ vimāḥ ādeśāt parameṣṭhinaḥ yāvat dattam kumārāya senāpatyam harāyā intum abhyāgataḥ tūrṇam kumāram nārakaḥ tadā āgatam tam tadā vīkṣya līlayā pārvatī sutaḥ ha dahati āśu mahā daityam tūlam vahniḥ iva āssve dagdhvā tu tārakam ghoram pataṃga mitra pātrakaḥ tatas prīta manāḥ skandaḥ mātuḥ aṅkam upāviśat mahādevaḥ api bhagavant vedha ādīn viṣṇunā saha iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde nārada indra saṃvādādikathana nāma triṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ kathitaḥ bhavartī sūta vivāhaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ tripuradviṣaḥ upāsitaḥ yatas samyak bhagavān bādarāyaṇaḥ tad prasādāt tvayā labdham jñānam tat pārameśvaram durlabham sarva śāstreṣu munīnām ca mahātmanām taḥ uvāca yat uktam brahmanā pūrve nāradāya mahātmane manasā tena tat śṛṇudhvam dvijottamāḥ satya loke sukha āsīnam brahmānam tejasām nidhim ṛṣibhiḥ munibhiḥ siddhaiḥ vedaiḥ sa aṅgaiḥ upāsitam saṃgīyamānam gandharvaiḥ stūyamānam marut gaṇaiḥ dṛṣṭvā praṇamya vidhivat nārada ratam atha abravīt nāradaḥ uvāca bhakti yogasya māhātmyam devadevasya śūlinaḥ praṇamya śaṃkaram śāntam aprameyam anāmayam bhakti yogam pravakṣyāmi śṛṇu nāradaiḥ suvrataiḥ bhakti yogasya māhātmyam yathā śambhoḥ mayā śrutam kathaṃcid yadi sā labdhā teṣām na eva asti durlabham viṣṇu tvam api muktim ca nūnam prāpnoti nāradaiḥ śubhānām aśubhānām ca karmaṇām rāśi saṃcayam na tad samamī caturvedī na agniṣṭoma ādi yajña kṛt śiva bhaktāḥ mahātmānaḥ mucyante te na saṃśayaḥ api duṣkṛta karmāṇaḥ prasādāt śūlinaḥ mune api aśvamedhāt adhikam phalam bhavati nāradaḥ jīvitam cañcalam jñātvā padma pattre iva udakam matim prakurvāṇaḥ saṃsārāt ati bhīṣaṇāt mucyate muni śārdūlaiḥ matiḥ śarve ati durlabhā bhava vyāla mukha sthānām bhīrūṇām dehinām mune tasmāt vimocakaḥ teṣām mahādevaḥ iti śrutiḥ tarati eva prasādāt parameṣṭhinaḥ svarga arthinām mumukṣūṇām brahmatvam api kāṅkṣiṇām bhaktiḥ eva virūpākṣe na anyaḥ pathī iti śrutiḥ sadā manīṣibhiḥ kāryā bhaktiḥ eva hi nāradaiḥ ca na sevyate śive dānam śive homaḥ śive snānam śive japaḥ akṣayāṇi phalāni eṣām iti āha bhagavant śivaḥ yat phalam naimiṣe tathā prayāge ca prabhāse ca gaṅgāsāgara saṃgame rudrakoṭau gayāyām ca śāligrāme amareśvare puṣkare bhārabhūteśe gokarṇe maṇḍaleśvare liṅge arcite akhilam viśvam arcitam syāt na saṃśayaḥ māyayā mohita ātmānaḥ na jānanti maheśvaram yaḥ pūjitam śivam dṛṣṭvā praṇamet bhakti bhāvāt ye punar śānta manasaḥ śiva bhaktāḥ jita indriyāḥ pṛthivyām yāni tīrthāni puṇyāni āyatanāni ca hi śiva liṅge vasanti eva tāni sarvāṇi nāradaiḥ tasmāt liṅga sadā pūjyam bhakti bhāvena nityaśas yaḥ tu liṅga arcanam tyaktvā devān anyān ca pūjayet ratnam vihāya mūḍha ātmā yathā kācam apekṣate caturdaśyām atha aṣṭamyām paurṇamāsyām tathā eva ca amāvāsyā ūm trayodaśyām pūjayet induśekharam sa snātaḥ sarva tīrtheṣu sarva yajñeṣu dīkṣitaḥ śiva arcana rataḥ nityam mahāpātaka sambhavaiḥ darśanāt śiva bhaktānām sakṛt sambhāṣaṇāt api brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyaḥ vaiśyaḥ śūdraḥ vā antyaja jāti jaḥ api parīkṣeta na kulam na vratam tathā tripuṇḍra aṅkita bhālena pūjyaḥ eva hi nārada tu bhaktān vinindati niraya aniṣkṛtiḥ na asti tasya mūḍha ātmanaḥ mune hitvā śiva bhaktān varjayitvā sarveṣām śāsakaḥ yamaḥ na śiva āśrayiṇaḥ maujī na daṇḍaḥ na ca kuṇḍale na eva kāṣāya vāsāṃsi bhaktiḥ eva atra kāraṇam yadi bhaktāḥ paśupatau pāpa karmasu ye ratāḥ punar martya dharma samāsādya vijñeyāḥ te gaṇeśvarāḥ yamāt bhayam na tasya asti rāja ca eva tu kā kathā māścaryaiḥ kathayiṣyāmi śṛṇu nāradaiḥ yat purā ujjayinyām nṛpaḥ hi āsīt nāmnā satyadhvajaḥ mune tatparaḥ dharma ātmā satya saṃkalpaḥ prajā pālana tatparaḥ bhuktvā samastām avanim kālena atha divam gataḥ mahākāla arcana rataḥ tad niṣṭhaḥ tad parāyaṇaḥ na dharmeṇa prajāḥ śāsti rāja dharma bahiṣkṛtaḥ asādhūn saṃparityajya sādhūn vai hanti asau nṛpaḥ prajānām kuśalam na asti sarvatra paripanthinaḥ yajñaḥ ca yajvanām dṛṣṭvā mlecchāḥ vidhvaṃsayanti tān mṛtyu kālaḥ atha saṃprāptaḥ dehinām ati bhīṣaṇaḥ pāpiṣṭhaḥ iti tam matvā saṃprāptāḥ yama kiṃkarāḥ śiva bhaktaḥ iti prāptāḥ tri netrāḥ śūla dhāriṇaḥ hi śiva dūtaiḥ samānītam vimānam sārvakāmikam hartum udyatāḥ sarve nṛpam tam yama kiṃkarāḥ gaṇeśvarāḥ tatas kruddhāḥ dṛṣṭvā tān yama kiṃkarān tāḍayitvā bhṛśam dūtān yama śāsana pālakān mahā kiṃkarāḥ ūcuḥ harmaiḥ yathā vṛttam īśvarasya gaṇeśvaraiḥ śṛṇu dharmaiḥ yathā vṛttam īśvarasya gaṇeśvaraiḥ sarva anara mari tāḍayitvā nītaḥ pāpaḥ vasuśrutaḥ na dharmeṇa prajāḥ pāti katham śiva puram gataḥ tasmāt bravīhi bharata vā ājñā kāriṇaḥ vayam evam teṣām vacaḥ śrutvā dharmarāj sūrya nandanaḥ vacaḥ provāca gambhīram nāradaiḥ deva asura manuṣyāṇām sarveṣām prāṇinām api hantā aham na asti saṃdehaḥ śiva bhaktam ṛte kila māhātmyam śiva bhaktānām kaḥ vā vindati tattvāt teṣām niyantā bhagavant mahādevaḥ na ca aparaḥ śiva bhaktāḥ mahātmānaḥ sadā śarva arcane ratāḥ api āśrama ācāra hīnān tyajadhvam tān prayatnāt varṇa āśramāṇām ācārāḥ api tena vivarjitāḥ śaṃkare yadi bhaktaḥ syāt na śāsyaḥ pūjyaḥ eva hi bhavadbhiḥ parihartavyāḥ śiva bhaktāḥ prayatnāt bibhemi śiva bhaktebhyaḥ siṃhāt iva yathā mṛgāḥ śveta raya āharaṇe pūrvam aham devena ghātitaḥ tatas prabhṛti aham śāratā tad bhaktānām na kiṃkarāḥ yaḥ asau vasu śrutaḥ rājā na prajāḥ pālayan yadi tathā api śaṃkare bhaktaḥ manas vāc kāya karmabhiḥ sādāttasya devasya pāpam spṛśati tam katham yaḥ devam mahākālam tam īśvaram bhavet varṣa koṭi śatam divyam śiva loke mahīyate candanāt cīgaroḥ jñeyam puṇyam aṣṭaguṇa adhikam bhṛṣṇagaroḥ viśeṣeṇa dviguṇam phalam iṣyate tasmāt śataguṇam puṇyam kuṅkumasya vidhīyate liṅgam etaiḥ samālipya gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt saṃvījya tālavṛntena liṅgam gandhaiḥ su lepitam daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi śiva loke mahīyate mayūra vyajanam dadyāt śviāya atīva śobhanam varṣa koṭi śatam divyam śiva loke mahīyate mātṛ hā ityādi śloka sthāne ka kha ga jha saṃjñita pustakeṣu kiṃcid bhinnam śloka artham eva dṛśyate raktikā mātram pradattvā vā adhikam bhavet varṣa koṭi śatam divyam śiva loke mahīyate candanāt ca ogaroḥ jñeyam puṇyam aṣṭaguṇa adhikam bhṛṣṇagaroḥ viśeṣeṇa dviguṇam phalam iṣyate tasmāt śataguṇam puṇyam kuṅkumasya vidhīyate tat liṅgam etaiḥ samālipya gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt saṃvījya tālavṛntena liṅgam gandhaiḥ su lepitam daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi śiva loke mahīyate mayūra vyajanam dadyāt śviāya atīva śobhanam varṣa koṭi śatam divyam śiva loke mahīyate mātṛ hā ityādi śloka sthāne ka kha ga jha saṃjñita pustakeṣu kiṃcid bhinnam śloka artham eva dṛśyate raktikā mātram pradattvā vā adhikam bhavet varṣa koṭi śatam divyam śiva loke mahīyate candanācī garoḥ jñeyam puṇyam aṣṭaguṇa adhikam bhṛṣṇagaroḥ viśeṣeṇa dviguṇam phalam iṣyate tasmāt śataguṇam puṇyam kuṅkumasya vidhīyate liṅgam etaiḥ samālipya gāṇapatyam avāpnuyāt saṃvījya tālavṛntena liṅgam gandhaiḥ su leopitam daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi śiva loke mahīyate mayūra vyajanam dadyāt śivānyā atīva śobhanam varṣa koṭi śatam divyam śiva loke mahīyate mātṛ hā ityādi śloka sthāne ka kha ga jha saṃjñita pustakeṣu śloka artham eva dṛśyate cāmaram yaḥ śive dadyāt maṇi ratna vibhūṣitam hema rūpya ādi daṇḍam vā tasya puṇya phalam śṛṇu cāmara āsakta hastābhiḥ divya strī parivāritaḥ vimānam varam āruhya gaṇaiḥ yāti śivam padam araṇya sambhavaiḥ puṣpaiḥ pattraiḥ vā giri sambhavaiḥ mad ārāma udbhavaiḥ vā api puṣpaiḥ saṃpūjayet śivam bhavet puṇyam atha uttaram tapaḥ śīla guṇa āḍhyāya veda vedāṅga gāmine daśa dattvā suvarṇasya phalam hi tat avāpnuyāt arka puṣpaiḥ kṛtā pūjā yadi devāya śambhave arka puṣpa sahastrebhyaḥ śamī puṣpam viśiṣyate mā puṣpa sahasrebhyaḥ kuśa puṣpam viśiṣyate puṣpa sahastrebhyaḥ padma puṣpam viśiṣyate bṛhat puṣpa sahastrebhyaḥ droṇapuṣpam viśiṣyate apāmārga sahastrebhyaḥ śrīmat nīlotpalam varam sahasreṇa yaḥ mālām saṃprayacchati śivāya vidhivat bhaktyā tasya puṇya phalam śṛṇu ca vaset śiva pure śrīmān śiva tulya parākramaḥ karavīra samā jñeyā jātī vijayapāṭalā nāga campaka puṃnāgāḥ dhattūraka samāḥ smṛtāḥ randhukam ketakī puṣpam kunda yūthī madantikāḥ marīṣam ca arjunam puṣpam prayatnena vivarjayet kanakāni kadambāni rātrau deyāni śaṃkare divā śeṣāṇi puṣpāṇi divā rātrau ca mallikāḥ praharam tiṣṭhate jātī karavīram aharniśam ca puṣpāṇām api alābhe tu pattrāṇi api nivedayet phalānām api alābhe tu tṛṇa gulma auṣadhaiḥ api auṣadhānām abhāve tu bhaktyā bhavati pūjitaḥ dhattūrakaiḥ tu yaḥ liṅgam sakṛt pūjayate naraḥ vrajet mallikā utpala puṣpāṇi nāga puṃnāga campakaiḥ ca sa yat phalam avābhāti tat ekāgra manāḥ śṛṇu sūrya koṭi pratīkāśaiḥ vimānaiḥ sārvakāmikaiḥ puṣpa mālā parikṣikṣaiḥ gīta vāditra niḥsvanaiḥ akṣaya labhate lokān a tiraskṛta śāsanaḥ mahā ādi sarva lokeṣu yatra iṣṭam tatra yāti saḥ pūjā ādi bhakti vinyāsaiḥ arcana ādiṣu sarvatas phalam ekam samam jñeyam phalam vitta anusārāt svayam utpādya puṣpāṇi yaḥ svayam pūjayet śivam tāni sākṣāt pragṛhṇāti devadevaḥ maheśvaraḥ kṛṣṇāroḥ sa karpūra dhūpam dadyāt śivāya vai nairantaryeṇa māsa ardham tasya puṇya phalam śṛṇu kalpa koṭi sahasrāṇi kalpa koṭi śatāni ca bhuktvā śiva pure bhogān tad ante pṛthivīpatiḥ guggulam ghṛta saṃyuktam sākṣāt gṛhṇāti śaṃkaraḥ māsa ardham dhūpa dānena śiva loke mahīyate dahet sa yāti paramam sthānam yatra devaḥ pinākadhṛt hrīphalam ca ājya sammiśram dattvā anoti parām gatim ebhiḥ sugandhitaḥ dhūpaḥ ṣaṣ sahasra guṇa uttaraḥ śāli taṇḍula prasthena kuryāt anam susaṃskṛtam da tvā caturdaśyām viśeṣataḥ tāvat varṣa sahasrāṇi śiva loke mahīyate iti guḍa khaṇḍa ghṛtānām ca bhakṣyāṇām ca nivedanāt tu dattvā bhavet ghṛrta dīpa pradānena śivāya śata yojanam yaḥ kuryāt kārttike māsi śobhanām dīpa mālikām sūrya ayuta pratīkāśaḥ tejasā bhāsayan diśaḥ tejas rāśiḥ vimāna sthaḥ sūrya vat yotate sadā śirasā dhārayet dīpam sairva rātrau viśeṣataḥ lalāṭe vā atha hastābhyām śirasā vā atha nāradaiḥ sūrya ayuta pratīkāśaiḥ vimānaiḥ sārvakāmikaiḥ candra aṃśu nirmalaḥ śrīmān subhagaḥ kāma rūpa dhṛt kṛtvā pradakṣiṇam bhaktyā naraḥ tu śivāyatana karmaṇi upayuktāni bhūtāni khanana utpātana ādiṣu hi kāmatas akāmatas vā api sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca mahat śivam yānti na saṃdehaḥ prasādāt parameṣṭhinaḥ tad krośa mātram śiva kṣetram samantāt parameṣṭhinaḥ dehinām tatra pañcatvam śiva sāyujya kāraṇam manuṣya sthāpite liṅgaiḥ kṣetra mānam idam smṛtam pāpa ācāraḥ api yaḥ tatra pañcatvam yāti nāradaiḥ tasmāt āvasatham kuryāt śiva kṣetra samīpatas mahā gaṅgā iti saṃjñā iyam tatra snāna ādinā trajet yaḥ kuryāt adhikām vā api kūpam vā api śiva āśrame iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde pañcākṣaramanaprabhāvādikathanam nāma pañcaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ puṣpam vā yadi vā pattram sa kūliṅge samarpitam tuṣṭe śive padārtha kaḥ durlabhaḥ hi nṛṇām prabho yāvat dātum śivaḥ śaktaḥ tāvat cintayitum prabhuḥ ṛddhi siddhī na dūra sthe śiva prīti artha karmaṇām narāṇām naranāthe kim prīte tu durlabham bhavet viśveśvaram sadā premṇā ye bhajanti nara uttamāḥ śrī śambhu nātham bhuvi mānavāḥ ye bhajanti bhaktyā nara loka vandyāḥ bhavanti te hāṭaka pūrṇa gehāḥ deha avasāne śiva loka bhājaḥ brahmā vā surāpaḥ vā steyī vā gurutalpa gaḥ yaḥ antakāle śivam smaryāt śiva sāyujyam āpnuyāt nirmālyam dhārayet bhaktyā śirasā pārvatīpateḥ idam ślokā ka asti pustakau tasmāt ityādinā id iti antaḥ sa ardhaḥ śṭokaḥ na asti tuṣṭe śiva etyādi śiva loka bhājaḥ iti antam śloka pañca kagajajha saṃjñita pustakeṣu na asti tasya pāpāni naśyanti na atra kāryā vicāraṇā na spṛśet api pādena na spṛśet api pādena laṅghayena api nāradaiḥ nirmālya laṅghanāt śambhoḥ cāṇḍālaḥ saḥ abhijāyate pṛthūdakam mahat tīrtham gaṅgā ca yamunā tathā narmadā sarayū kṣiprā tathā godāvarī nadī sadā saṃnihitāḥ tu evam śambho snāna udeṃke mune śambhoḥ snāna udakam sevyam sarva tīrtha mayam hi tat dhāraṇāt pāpa saṃghātaiḥ tad kṣaṇāt eva mucyate na tān spṛśanti pāpāni manas vāc kāya jāni api nāradaḥ uvāca procyate tātaiḥ kena vā tat adhiṣṭhitam avyaktam ānandam tamasaḥ param mahādevasya yatnena liṅgī syāt tena śaṃkaraḥ ekārṇave purā ghore naṣṭaiḥ sthāvara jaṅgamaiḥ mama viṣṇoḥ pravodha artham āvirbhūtam śiva ātmakam tadā prabhṛtya viṣṇuḥ bhaktyā paramayā mudā liṅga mūrti dharam śāntam pūjayāvaḥ vṛṣadhvajam nāradaḥ uvāca kaḥ tvam kimartham vā śeṣe śīghram uttiṣṭha durmate evam mad vacanam śrutvā prahasan madhusūdanaḥ mām abravīt ameya ātmā katham garvāyase mudhā katamaḥ aham sarva lokānām pālakaḥ aham na saṃśayaḥ saṃhartā aham punar ca ante na anyaḥ asti sadṛśaḥ mayā evam vivāde saṃjāte mama devena śārṅgiṇā prādurbhūtam tadā liṅgam āvayoḥ darpa hāri tat tasmin liṅge mahādevaḥ svayam jyotīḥ sanātanaḥ sahasra śīrṣā puruṣaḥ sahasra akṣaḥ sahasrapād ardhanārīśvaraḥ anantaḥ tejorāśiḥ durāsadaḥ mad jyeṣṭha tvam vām tāvat āstām kiṃcid ravīmi aham mūlam mama asya liṅgasya yadi paśyati mādhavaḥ mad nūnam bhaviṣyati jyeṣṭhaḥ iti devena bhāṣitam evam śambhoḥ nigaditam urarīkṛtya nāradaiḥ gatam deva ṛṣe nūnam vismaya āviṣṭa cittayoḥ hariḥ mūlam a dṛṣṭvā eva tam devam punar āgataḥ tam eva śaraṇam gatvā saṃstūya vividhaiḥ stavaiḥ prītaḥ bhūtvā mahādevaḥ vākyam etat uvāca ha maheśvaraḥ uvāca mad bhaktānām tvam eva agryaḥ pūjyaḥ mānyaḥ tvam eva hi liṅge mām pūjaya hare liṅga mūrti dharaḥ hi aham liṅga ārādhanāt kṣipram ajñānam nāśayāmi aham liṅga arcana ratānām ca nāritaiḥ saṃsāra jam bhayam evam harevaram dattvā mām uvāca maheśvaraḥ gṛhāṇa caturaḥ vedān caturbhiḥ vadanaiḥ vidhe iti āvābhyām varam dattvā devadevaḥ pinākadhṛt viśveśvaraḥ svayam jyotīḥ kṣaṇāt antarhitaḥ abhavat tatas prabhṛti viṣṇu ādyāḥ devāḥ daityāḥ ca dānavāḥ gandharvāḥ munayaḥ siddhāḥ yakṣāḥ nāga aśva kiṃnarāḥ saṃpūjya paramam liṅgam parām siddhim gatāḥ mune jñātvā tvam evam devarṣe liṅga arcana rataḥ bhava treṣu ca eva tīrtheṣu vaneṣu upavaneṣu ca yāni liṅgāni divyāni sthāpitāni sura asuraiḥ nāradaḥ uvāca kāni sthānāni divyāni yeṣu saṃnihitaḥ śivaḥ mama brahman māhātmyam ca api kṛtsnaśas māhātmyam divya liṅgānām tīrthānām api nārada atra te kathayiṣyāmi śrūyatām agha śāsanam yā sā śaivī parā mūrtiḥ śiva bhaktyā pām patiḥ nārāyaṇaḥ svayam sākṣāt aham ca anyāḥ ca devatāḥ vasanti sāgare nūnam tīrtharāja iti saḥ smṛtaḥ mahā puṇyam tatra api lavaṇa udadhiḥ ahorātra kṛtam pāpam darśanāt eva naśyati spṛṣṭvā tri rātrakam pāpam nāśayati eva sāgaraḥ sapta rātra kṛtam pāpam prokṣaṇāt eva naśyati pānena pakṣa janitam snānāt pakṣa dvayasya ca tathā aṣṭamyām parvasnānam ca vārṣikam bhānau anudite nityam yaḥ snāti lavaṇodadhau kapilāyāḥ phalam tasya dattāyāḥ śrotriye dhruvam upoṣya rajanīm ekām ravi saṃkramaṇam prati dānāni yāni lokeṣu vikhyātāni manīṣibhiḥ teṣām phalam avāpnoti grahaṇe candra sūryayoḥ ca etāsām saṃgamaḥ yatra snānam kuryāt mahā udadhau yāni pāpāni ghorāṇi bhrūṇahatyā ādikāni ca nāśam yānti kṣaṇāt eva saṃgamasya prabhāvāt yatra siddhāḥ purā vatsaiḥ munayaḥ sapta koṭayaḥ saptakoṭīśvaram nāma tatas prabhṛti nārada mama nārāyaṇaḥ devaḥ śaśvandraḥ divākaraḥ marutaḥ munayaḥ siddhāḥ khecarāḥ bhūcarāḥ atha ye arcayitvā param liṅgam saptakoṭīśvaram śivam prāptavantaḥ parām siddhim tasmin liṅge ca nāradaiḥ iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure śivārcanamāhātmyādikathanam nāma ṣaṭṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ ujjayinyām mahā kālam ye vai paśyanti mānavāḥ avāpnuyuḥ param lokam yatra gatvā na śocati sparśanāt tasya liṅgasya sa śarīrāḥ śivam yayuḥ tat jñātvā ca mayā tatra pāṣāṇaḥ kukkuṭa ākṛtiḥ nikṣiptaḥ ca mahākāle tatas abhūt kukkuṭeśvaraḥ śūleśvarasya pūrve tu oṃkāram liṅgam uttamam snānam samācaran tatra prayata ātmā samāhitaḥ dvitīye ahani tṛtīye ahani daśame vā api nāradaiḥ pakṣe māse atha ṣaṣ māse svame paśyati śaṃkaram jñānam avāpnoti devānām api durlabham yaḥ paśyet liṅgam oṃkāram snātvā kuṇḍe samāhitaḥ dīkṣā sahasrasya phalam prāpya yāti parām gatim tatra eva agastya muninā tapasā ārādhitaḥ śivaḥ prādurbhūtaḥ ca bhagavān agastyeśvara nāmnaḥ tatra snātvā bhagavat am yaḥ tu paśyati mānavaḥ tīrthāni koṭiśas santi ujjayinyām samantataḥ teṣām māhātmyam akhilam skānde skandena bhāṣitam maheśvaraḥ tatra āssīt pulahaḥ sthāṇu mandire tad ante mad sutaḥ jātaḥ sthāṇu mūḍhaiḥ prabhāvāt yaj sakṛt ca manujaḥ śaivam padam avāpnuyāt tīrtharājaḥ iti khyātaḥ prayāgaḥ muni sattamāḥ tatra snātvā divam gatvā bhogān bhuktvā yathā īpsayā maheśvaraḥ yatra sarva anugrāhakaḥ paraḥ darśanāt akṣaya ālokān prāpnoti manuja uttamaḥ anya tīrtham param guhyam gayātīrtham iti smṛtam pitṝṇām akṣayā tṛptiḥ tatra piṇḍa dānāt mahānadyām naraḥ snātvā rudrapādam spṛśet yadi mahākālam mahā tīrtha kāla kālasya vallabham tatra snātvā tu medhāvī caraṇam pārvatīpateḥ yaḥ paśyati naraḥ bhaktyā śaivam padam avāpnuyāt prāyas prāntam upoṣyam syāt tīrthe deva phala īpsubhiḥ mūlam hi pitṛ tuṣṭi arthaiḥ pitryam ca uktam mahā ṛṣibhiḥ yām prāpya astam upaiti arkaḥ sā ced syāt tri muhūrtikā dharma kṛtyeṣu sarveṣu saṃpūrṇām tām viduḥ tithim aṣṭamī ekādaśī ṣaṣṭhī tṛtīyā ca caturdaśī kartavyā para saṃyuktā a parā pūrva miśritā tathā rambhā sāvitrī vaṭapaitṛkī kṛṣṇa aṣṭamī ca sa bhūtā kartavyā sammukhā tithiḥ siddha pratiṣṭhite liṅge na caṇḍasya adhikārāt svayam cāndrāyaṇa samam puṇyam śambho naivedya bhakṣaṇāt vṛṣam caṇḍam nṛpam caitra somasūtram punarvaṣam caṇḍam ca somasūtram ca punar caṇḍam punarvaṣam āram ca āranālam ca masūrikā caṇakāḥ tila tailam ca mantra vīrya harāṇi paṭ vāma pārśve vinikṣipya gṛhītvā vāma pāṇinā dhṛtvā ca dakṣiṇe pāṇau taile dadyāt jala añjalim labhet ubhayayoḥ saṃdhyayoḥ apaḥ tris kṣipet asura kṣayāt praṇāmam eka hastena ekam vā api pradakṣiṇam tathā akāle abda puṇyam vinaśyati sabhāyām yajña śālāyām devatāyatane gurau pratyekam ca namaskāraḥ hanti puṇyam purā kṛtam eva ete ca eva akṣāragaṇāḥ anye kṣāragaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ makṣikāḥ maśakāḥ veśyāḥ yācakāḥ ca eva mūṣakāḥ gaṇakāḥ grāmaṇīcā eva saptā ete parabhakṣakāḥ iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde tithinirṇayādikathanam nāma aṣṭaṣaṣṭitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ nāradaḥ uvāca hetunā kena bhagavant kāla kālaḥ maheśvaraḥ āsīt muni varaḥ pūrva nāmnā śvetaḥ iti smṛtaḥ tīrtha udakāni seveta yamān ca niyamān tathā māheśvara agraṇī śāntaḥ mahādeva arcane rataḥ tam netum āgataḥ kālaḥ daṇḍa hastaḥ bhayaṃkaraḥ dṛṣṭvā kālam saḥ vipra indraḥ bhaya vyākulita indriyaḥ spṛṣṭvā karābhyām tat liṅgam dhyāyamānaḥ maheśvaram prahasan abravīt kālaḥ śvetam muni varam mune tīrtha dānam praśaṃsanti niratāḥ sveṣu karmasu yajanti mad bhayāt devān yajñān ca vividhān tathā tasmāt uttiṣṭha neṣyāmi mama pāśa vaśam gataḥ na eva paśyanti te adya muni puṃgavāḥ atha abravīt yamam bhītaḥ pāśa haratam karāliṇam katham īśa arcana ratam tvam mām netum iha arhasi vada pāśaiḥ dṛdataraiḥ śīghram dhyāyamānam maheśvaram tam dṛṣṭvā devadeveśam prahṛṣṭaḥ abhūt tadā muniḥ haraḥ atha abravīt kālam mama bhaktam vimocaya akarot bhara masāt kālam śvetaḥ pāśaiḥ vimocitaḥ hattam bhagavantā tasmai gāṇapatyam ca śāśvatam devyā saha mahādevaḥ kṣaṇāt antarhitaḥ abhavat anena hetunā śambhuḥ kāla kālaḥ iti smṛtaḥ aham ca viṣṇunā sārdham stutvā devam maheśvaram prasādya atha punar jātaḥ kālaḥ śambho anugrahāt puṇyatamam jvāleśvaram iti smṛtam revā tīre muni śreṣṭhaiḥ mahāpātaka nāśanam koṭiśas santi tīrthāni tasmin jvāleśvare śive tatra snātvā deva ṛṣe dṛṣṭvā jvāleśvaram śivam mahīyate sadā saṃnihitaḥ śambhu liṅge śrī mallikārjune manuṣyāḥ paśavaḥ koṭi mṛga aśva maśaka ādayaḥ mṛtāḥ sarve yānti śambhoḥ param padam paramam tīrtham priyam devasya śūlinaḥ tatra snātvā udakam pītvā saṃpūjya ca pinākinam vṛṣadhvaje param tīrthaiḥ devikāyāḥ taṭe mune yatra snātvā śivam dṛṣṭvā brahma hatyām vyapohati godāvarī nadī yatra nirgatā pāpa hāriṇī tatra snānam japaḥ dānam brahmayajña makhaḥ kṛtaḥ tatra snātvā śivam dṛṣṭvā devadevam tryambakam revāyāḥ na ati dūre tu gokarṇaḥ iti viśrutaḥ tatra saṃnihitaḥ śivaḥ niyataḥ aniyataḥ vā api yaḥ vā kaḥ vā api mānavaḥ devasya vāyu diś bhāge deveśī bhadrakālikā yoga siddhi pradā nityam darśanāt prāṇinām mune mahā balaḥ ca bhagavān yatra āsste girijāpatiḥ maheśvaraḥ tasya darśana mātreṇa rājasūya phalam labhet anyat dāru vanam puṇyam śaṃkarasya ati vallabham teṣām tena dhūmena mahatā vyāptaḥ brahmāṇḍa maṇḍapaḥ śambhogā devī dhūma vyāptam jagatrayam dṛṣṭvā pamaccha viśveśam kautukāt īśvara īśvarā dhūmasya kāraṇam brūhi devadevaiḥ maheśvaraiḥ maheśvaraḥ uvāca yatra dāru vanam puṇyam mama ca atīva vallabham tatra tiṣṭhanti munayaḥ tapas niṣṭhāḥ jita indriyāḥ a viditvā eva mām devi śarīra kleśa kāriṇi teṣām mūrdhani sthitaḥ bhṛgaḥ sacarācaram karmāṇi yāni lokeṣu puṣkalāni bahūni ca sarvāṇi niṣphalāni eva mām a jñātvā eva pārvati evam devasya vacanam śrutvā śamathā bravīt devadeva mahādeva munīnām bhāvitātmanām ajñānasya yathā vyāptiḥ tām aham draṣṭum utsahe evam devyāḥ vacaḥ śrutvā bhagavant nīlalohitaḥ strī rūpa dhārī viṣṇuḥ ca śaṃkareṇa samāgataḥ viṣṇunā saha devadāru vanaukasaḥ mohayan māyayā śambhuḥ vicacāra vane tadā muni striyaḥ śivam dṛṣṭvā madana anala dīpitāḥ tyakta lajjāḥ vivastrāḥ vai yayuḥ tāḥ anu śaṃkaram strī rūpa dhāriṇam viṣṇum sarve muni kumārakāḥ anvagacchanta deva ṛṣe kāma vāṇa prapīḍitāḥ tat adbhutam tadā jñātvā kupitāḥ munayaḥ tadā liṅga hīnam haram kṛtvā harim tadā prabhṛti vimā indra śivā mekhala saṃjñitā saṃyogaḥ sarva pāpa haraḥ śivaḥ iti śrutvā tu devarṣiḥ brahmanaḥ vacanam tadā jagāma kartu tīrthāni śiva bhakti puraskṛtaḥ etat saram purāṇam te yathāvat samudīritam kiṃtu mayā āgā ādyaiḥ kim yajñaiḥ bhūri dakṣiṇaiḥ tu ogi indrāḥ kim tena sadṛśam bhavet bhaktaḥ niyataḥ śṛṇuyāt idam brāhma pāśava bhaktān atha puraskṛtya samāhitaḥ phalam ye pūjayet rācakam naraḥ viśveśvaraḥ mahādevaḥ prīyatām iti bhāvaḥ tatra dattā bhūmiḥ śiva arthinā sā ātārayati dātuḥ hi pūrvajān sakalān api śrutvā grantham imam samyak dadyāt dānāni śaktitas tāni akṣaya phalāni āhuḥ munayaḥ veda vādinaḥ iti śrī brahmapurāṇa upapurāṇe śrī saure sūta śaunaka saṃvāde śivatīrtha kathanam munipatnīmohanam nāma ekonasaptati namas adhyāyaḥ
